Current Affairs Commentary

League of Nations Mediation of the Sino-Japanese Dispute 35

丨What Will Be the Result?丨

(I) The End of the Road for [Reasoning]

Since the September 18th Incident, our country has been enduring and yielding, attempting to accommodate the so-called peace and justice. The price our people have paid for peace cannot be considered small, and the sacrifices made for justice cannot be considered few. As for the three northeastern provinces, extending to Yuguan, the land area is at least 3.78 million square kilometers. The population is over 30 million. The loss of life due to the Japanese military's atrocities is no less than 300,000. Property losses (since our government lacks statistics in this regard) are estimated to exceed 100 million yuan. Based on this, it cannot be said that our country's sincerity for peace and justice is not sufficient. However, how have we been rewarded? We still remember last December, when the League of Nations General Assembly, the proposals of the four countries of Czechoslovakia, Sweden, Ireland, and Spain showed definite recognition of fairness and justice, which was a voice of hope in these times dominated by iron fists. The most important point of the draft proposal submitted by the Committee of Nineteen to the Extraordinary Assembly on the 6th is that both factually and legally, it opposes the recognition of [Manchukuo]. However, at the same time, in order to accommodate Japan, it considers it impossible to restore the situation before the September 18th Incident. This kind of proposal seems beneficial to us on the surface. [Justice and peace] seem to have won a paper victory. However, we cannot be satisfied with this, and we deeply regret that the League of Nations has over-accommodated Japan's so-called facts. What is even worse is that on the 6th, discussions had reached a stage where points of agreement were emerging, but on the 8th, drafting was not even started, and the atmosphere at the meeting was extremely depressed, awaiting the development of Japan's new proposal. Currently, the three northeastern provinces are being ravaged, blood is being shed at Shanhaiguan, and Rehe is about to suffer the ravages of war. Regardless of all this, the main content of the so-called new proposal can be summarized as follows:

First, to seek mediation based on the spirit of the Lytton Report.

Second, the basis of mediation must first acknowledge [Manchukuo (puppet state)]. [Japan is even touting the absurd theory of Sino-Japanese-Manchu cooperation].

Third, mediation procedures must be based on the Drummond-Sugimura case.

Otherwise, Japan will appeal to the [world public] to seek a [public trial], etc. Alas, is Japan's so-called [public] the aristocracy in the eyes of Japanese militarists, or the blind masses completely anesthetized by Japanese militarism? If not, then there is probably no one else in the world who sincerely approves of the imperialistic monopoly and aggression and aids in cruel killings. However, the League of Nations Covenant clearly states that [war] cannot be used to affect international peace, and the [Kellogg-Briand Pact] also states that any international dispute cannot be [resolved] by means of [war]. However, Japan's invasion of the Northeast, the disturbance of Shanghai, the forcible seizure of Yuguan, and the bombing of Rehe are all [wars]. Each and every one demonstrates the violence of its army and navy. The League of Nations is deaf to this. What is the reason for not seeing with its eyes? It is merely because the two major powers of Britain and France are too concerned about friendly relations with Japan and value their immediate gains, and have forgotten the fact that our country is being invaded.

(II) What Good Is Speaking of Justice When Great Armies Are Pressing the Border?

We deeply respect the Allied nations in the League of Nations that advocate restraining violence with justice, such as the Czech Republic, Sweden, and Ireland. However, they are all small and weak, and the road is long and out of reach. Even if the League of Nations General Assembly accepts their proposals, it may not be able to stop the armed aggression of Japanese militarists. Moreover, the League of Nations was originally a tool used by the two major powers of Britain and France, and it has little to do with justice, fairness, and peace. Therefore, from the beginning, the peaceful resolution of the Sino-Japanese dispute has been a kind of [perfunctory peace]. In a word, it is [no determination to restrain Japan]. Although the League of Nations has indeed made every effort to accommodate and do its best as a mediator, how has Japan repaid the League of Nations? On the one hand, it says that the League of Nations is a European League of Nations. From the military department, which holds real political power, to the financial and capital cliques, and even the scholars employed by the government, all have the same opinion. It vigorously advocates its Pan-Asian Monroe Doctrine. Furthermore, it says that Manchuria has a special relationship with Japan, which the League of Nations has never understood. As a result, the Shenyang Incident has spread to northern Manchuria, and recently the disaster has affected Rehe, involving Tianjin and Peiping. If this continues, Japan will definitely not stop until it has completely annexed China. Therefore, we say that the major powers of the League of Nations, due to their own interests, have no determination to restrain Japan's atrocities, and the Japanese militarists are well aware of the world's trends. They are unwilling to swallow China whole, but instead adopt a gradual policy of encroachment, with the aim of deceiving the world and playing with the League of Nations. Japan's true intention is not necessarily to have the League of Nations recognize the [Manchukuo (puppet state)] that it created. What it desires is to delay the matter in fact, so as to facilitate the expansion of its invasion network. The member states of the League of Nations should not be deluded by the [open door, equal opportunity] that the Japanese militarists advocate in words. They must be prepared for the fact that in a few years, the three northeastern provinces will truly be annexed by Japan, and the balance of power in the Far East will be completely broken by Japan.

Our country is currently facing [countless difficulties], and past failures cannot be denied. Even if we want to give up everything to seek an intangible peace, we cannot. Japan has amassed great armies, such as the Eighth Division, Tenth Division, Fourteenth Division, Twentieth Division, Nineteenth Division, First Cavalry Brigade, and other special units. Even [first-year soldiers] have been conscripted to the Rehe border. It is estimated that the number of people is no less than 100,000. Their desire to take advantage of the opportunity is obvious. This kind of barbaric action cannot be deterred by a resolution from the League of Nations by Lake Geneva. What do we get from [self-consolation with empty words]? Today, disaster is imminent, and it is impossible to live in peace and tranquility. How can we allow ourselves to live in humiliation? For the sake of our nation's survival, we must risk everything and fight to the death as a last resort.

New World Flight Record 75

The British King and Prime Minister Send Telegrams to Congratulate the British Aviator on Success

French and American Aviators Will Hasten to Catch Up

(Marseilles, 9th) French renowned aviators Bossoutrot and Rossi are striving to grasp the world record for the longest distance around-the-world flight. The two once flew 6,587 miles. Now, British Air Force officers Gayford and Nicholetts have broken this record by flying a straight-line distance of 5,340 miles in 57 hours and 25 minutes. Today, it is heard that the aforementioned two French aviators plan to immediately start a straight-line flight to compete with Gayford and others.

According to news from Cape Town, Gayford and others' aircraft landed at Walvis Bay in southwest Africa last night, which is 5,340 miles from the starting point, Cranwell Aerodrome, and only 850 miles from Cape Town. Originally, they intended to reach their destination in one go, but due to poor atmospheric conditions, they had to land during the day out of caution. After landing, the two aviators immediately went to a hotel to get a full night's sleep. The two are energetic and well-groomed, not at all like people who have been in the air for 57 hours.

According to Gayford's report to the Air Ministry, the weather was clear along the way. It was not until they reached Nigeria that they encountered heavy fog, which hindered the flight. Mount Cameroon, at 13,000 feet, was completely obscured by clouds. During a heavy rainstorm on the second night, the sky was cloudy, and the automatic controller lost its effectiveness due to the adverse weather conditions, so it was not used afterward.

The journey was approximately nearly 6,000 miles, with an originally planned average speed of 93.3 miles per hour, but due to the obstacles encountered in Nigeria, the speed had to exceed 100 miles per hour.

The British King, Prime Minister MacDonald, Air Minister Londonderry, and the Air Defence Committee have all sent telegrams of congratulations. Pole Llewellyn B. Bubb, who with Boardman established a new record of 5,012 miles for long-distance flight from New York to Constantinople in 1931 (Boardman is American), also sent a congratulatory telegram, stating that he and his colleague Boardman will attempt to recover the lost record soon. This is because Boardman's record has also been broken by Gayford and Nicholetts' new record of 5,340 miles. (Reuters)

Britain Holds Three Major World Aviation Records 81

London, Reuters, 8th The Air Ministry issued a statement today announcing the success of the long-distance flight. It also stated that Britain now holds three major world aviation records: speed, distance, and altitude.

Altitude: In September 1932, Captain Uwins in Bristol ascended to 43,996 feet (over 8 miles).

Long Distance: The new record created by Captain Gayford and Air Lieutenant Nicholetts this time.

London, Reuters, 8th The British debt to the United States currently totals approximately US$4,500,000,000. Senator Borah stated today that he would fully oppose any cash settlement method that does not include commercial concessions. American Proposition 90

Washington, National News Agency, 8th Although factions within the U.S. Congress who firmly oppose revising or canceling war debts are still active at this time, many more members are seriously considering two major points of organizing war debts. It is reported that a portion of senators believe a clear distinction should be made within the war debts between funds used for wartime destructive actions and funds used for post-war relief, reconstruction, and the purchase of necessities. These groups also believe that prior to resolving the war debts, the currency prices of major debtor nations must first be stabilized and methods must be adopted to prevent the dumping of goods from countries with the lowest currency prices in order to hope for successful modification of the war debt agreements. According to several congressmen, the main obstacle to modifying war debts at present is the extreme devaluation of currencies, which has led to a sharp increase in the exports of nations. Friends of President Hoover have also voiced identical opinions today, stating that President Hoover believes that the current decline in global prices is due to currency devaluation. This issue must be dealt with quickly and effectively, after which the economy will have hope for recovery. Renay, chairman of the House Ways and Means Committee, also stated that he is unwilling to pay attention to any war debt modification proposal that does not include organizing currency prices and other factors that hinder the advancement of commerce. As Renay is known as a leader of the faction opposing discussion of war debt modification, the public believes Renay's attitude has made a noticeable concession. However, Renay still opposes the method of settling with a lump sum, especially opposing the issuance of such bonds in the United States, stating that he believes this method is meaningless. Senator Borah, who has always advocated complete cancellation of war debts, has also reiterated his position, stating that if the current issues restricting international trade are not organized first, then proceeding directly with canceling the war debts would not be helpful to either the debtor nations or the United States. As for the lump-sum settlement method, it will also not necessarily bring permanent benefits, because we must first find markets and restore the purchasing power of the people, and then can war debts be satisfactorily organized.

Japan's Enormous Budget 96

Parties Fear Offending Military, Decide to Agree Conditionally

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th—The deliberations of the House of Representatives' Budget Subcommittee concluded yesterday. To decide their stance on the budget proposal, the Seiyukai Party held a joint meeting of executives and budget committee members at the Shiba San'entei this morning. The Minseito Party and the Kokumin Domei Party also held discussions within the Diet. As each faction intends to approve the proposal without amendments, after the discussions and decisions by the subcommittees this morning, the final budget plenary session will be held at 2:00 PM to make a final decision. It is anticipated that the budget proposal will be submitted to the main session at 1:00 PM on the 13th for discussion and passage.

Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 9th—Japanese political parties held representative meetings today to discuss their stance on the military budget. It is reported that the Seiyukai Party has decided not to make any amendments but will unanimously pass it with the following hopes: (1) [Financial Issues] The government must fundamentally address national defense issues and reorganize the financial and tax systems to ensure financial stability. (2) [Industrial Issues] The government should promote industry, stabilize exchange rates, implement low-interest rate policies, and pursue inflationary policies to facilitate the smooth flow of capital in the financial sector. (3) [Other] It is deeply hoped that the government will take a fair stance in resolving the Meiji Sugar tax evasion issue and devise caring countermeasures.

The Minseito Party's representative meeting also resolved to pass the budget proposal without attaching conditions. Their key hopes are as follows: 1. Implement market control policies to prevent inflationary policies from becoming extreme and guard against exchange rate declines. 2. To consolidate finances, the government must reorganize the financial and tax systems. 3. For deficit bonds, a separate fixed source of revenue must be found as a debt repayment fund to maintain the credit of public bonds.

The demands of the two parties are not significantly different. The massive new budget is likely to pass safely through the Lower House on February 13. Japanese political parties dare not express the slightest dissent towards the new budget for fear of offending the military, which might prevent them from gaining power in the future.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 9th—At 2:30 PM today, the Kokumin Domei Party held a meeting of Diet members to exchange opinions on the budget proposal. The results of the discussion were as follows: The government budget is fundamentally contrary to the Kokumin Domei's economic policies, but in light of the current situation, it is conditionally approved. Furthermore, at the main session on the 13th, Kato Choichi and Koyamadani Zo will take the stage to explain the party's position in detail and express their support.

Japanese Naval Airship Crashes into Sea 97

Japan United News Agency, Tokyo, 9th—The Tateyama Naval Air Station conducted a night flight training exercise starting at 5:00 PM on the 8th. Among the crew members, three are missing. The Japanese Navy has three Type 90 airships, one of which was destroyed in Tateyama Bay during a typhoon last autumn. This is the second loss.

Japan's Total Debt 98

Totaling 1.8 Billion Yen

Reuters, Tokyo, 9th—According to a survey by the Bank of Japan, Japan's foreign debt at the end of 1932 amounted to 1,896,920,664 yen, with annual interest payments of 114,102,076 yen. The foreign debt includes 85,470,235 pounds sterling, 203,799,300 US dollars, 41,623,500 francs, and 4,000,000 South Manchurian Railway bonds.

Blood Brotherhood Reveals Inside Story (Japan Communication) 99

Japan's expansion of territory, its conquests, whether viewed from a nationalistic or capitalistic standpoint, cannot be denied as a blessing to the Japanese Empire. Why then do cries of "national crisis" resound throughout Japan? The proliferation of the leftist Communist Party within Japanese society undoubtedly poses a significant danger, threatening to fundamentally destabilize Japan. However, the Communist Party has always been an illegal entity, subject to severe crackdowns by the police and oppression by various right-wing groups, including the veterans' associations. Therefore, while the Communist Party is indeed a serious problem in Japan and poses various obstacles to the rule of the Japanese militarists, its practical manifestations, at most, only present a threat to the Japanese imperialist regime, a mere ideological threat with no actual rebellious actions sufficient to endanger Japanese politics. Where, then, does the so-called national crisis lie?

Everyone knows that since Japan abandoned the gold standard and adopted an "inflationary policy," industry seems to have been slightly invigorated by rising prices. However, the general populace has suffered even greater hardships due to these rising prices. Consequently, cries of "economic downturn" are heard everywhere in the cities, and the plight of the rural areas worsens daily. The pressure of difficult living conditions has left the masses of farmers barely able to breathe. Therefore, people of all persuasions, whether leftist or rightist (excluding the ruling military elite and a small number of aristocrats), express extreme dissatisfaction with the current state of affairs.

This dissatisfaction with the status quo is prevalent among the general population and even among junior officers in the active-duty army and navy. Among these groups, the most formidable and potent collective force is the Blood Brotherhood. Over the past year, the "Blood Brotherhood" has indeed been a monster in Japan, an enigma difficult for Japanese society to decipher. Although we know that this is a right-wing group, a collective operating under the direction of the military, its content and actions are unknown to the general public.

Unknown to most, the central figure leading the Blood Brotherhood is a Buddhist monk. Under his guidance, in addition to those directly involved in action, there are many active-duty junior officers from the army and navy. Therefore, their tools have a source, and their comrades have safe places to hide. The leader of the Blood Brotherhood, named Inoue Akira (also known as Nissho), has as its core tenet of unity:

"The current state of our country (Japan) has many shortcomings in terms of ideology, economy, and other institutions. Political parties, financial cliques, and other privileged classes collude with each other, satisfying their selfish desires and pursuing their private interests, thereby neglecting the great cause of national survival and disrupting national governance. Therefore, we must seek its reform..."

Such statements have resonated with a segment of the population, evoking sympathy among a portion of the youth. In a Japanese society long accustomed to peace and plagued by economic hardship, it can indeed spark a kind of rebellious action. Thus, last year, during the height of the Shanghai War and as the election campaign was about to begin, former Finance Minister Inoue Junnosuke was suddenly assassinated. Barely a month later, Mitsui's loyal servant, Baron Dan Takuma, was also assassinated. Prime Minister Inukai Tsuyoshi was even killed at his official residence. All of these incidents are directly related to the Blood Brotherhood. Moreover, their planned killings were not limited to these numbers. According to the Japanese government's publicly released information, the list of figures the Blood Brotherhood intended to assassinate is as follows:

Assassinated:

Inukai Tsuyoshi (Former President of the Seiyukai Party, Former Prime Minister)

Inoue Junnosuke (Former Finance Minister, Executive of the Minseito Party)

Dan Takuma (Loyal Servant of Mitsui, Financial Clique)

Not Yet Assassinated:

Saionji Kinmochi (Duke, Elder Statesman)

Shidehara Kijuro (Former Foreign Minister, Son-in-Law of Mitsubishi)

Makino Nobuaki (Current Lord Keeper of the Privy Seal)

Suzuki Kisaburo (Current President of the Seiyukai Party, Former Home Minister)

Tokonami Takejiro (Elder Statesman of the Seiyukai Party, Former Railway Minister, Home Minister)

Wakatsuki Reijiro (Former President of the Minseito Party, Former Prime Minister)

Maeda Toshisada (Count, Elder Statesman, Former Minister of Agriculture and Commerce)

Tokugawa Iesato (Duke, President of the House of Peers)

Ikeda Seihin (Director of Mitsui)

Go Seinosuke (President of Tokyo Electric Light Company, Member of the House of Peers)

Mitsui Hachiroemon (Baron, Representative of Mitsui Gomei)

Kimura Hisayata (Executive Director of Mitsubishi Goshi)

Kagami Kenkichi (President of Nippon Yusen, Member of the Mitsubishi Board of Directors)

Iwasaki Koyata (Baron, President of Mitsubishi Goshi)

Sumitomo Kichizaemon (Baron, President of Sumitomo Goshi)

Okura Kihachiro (Baron, President of Okura Gumi)

Yasuda Zenjiro (President of Yasuda Shoji)

The above twenty individuals were the targets of the Blood Brotherhood's assassination plot. However, in reality, only three were killed before their leader was arrested. But their method involved one comrade killing one of their "targets." Although fourteen people have now been arrested, the foundations they secretly planted in the army, navy, and general society still exist, and their background has not been eliminated. It is feared that the unrest in Japanese society will not necessarily turn from danger to safety due to the arrest of a portion of the Blood Brotherhood. Moreover, the military is "exhausting its resources in military pursuits," sending people to the front lines in waves, further exacerbating the people's suffering. (February 4, Tokyo)

Wang Faqin Returns to Beijing 101

Feng Yuxiang Resolves to Resist Japan, Will Come to Beijing Soon

Special Envoy Huang Shaogu Informs the Central Government of His Opinions

North China's Situation Becomes Increasingly Urgent, Military and Civilians Unite in Resistance

Mr. Wang Faqin, specially appointed by the Central Government to go to Zhangjiakou to urge Feng Yuxiang to come to Beijing to jointly resist foreign aggression, returned to Beijing from Ping at 8:00 AM on the 8th. Accompanying him was Huang Shaogu, Feng Yuxiang's representative. After entering the city, they did not stay at the Central Hotel. Central figures such as Zhang Ji, Liu Shouzhong, and Zhao Piqian all visited them. In the afternoon, an important discussion was held. According to Mr. Wang's account of the situation in North China and Feng Yuxiang's attitude, he stated briefly: 1. Mr. Feng expressed to me that as long as the Central Government resists violence and relieves the national crisis, he is willing to make any sacrifice. Because he was originally a Central Committee member, a National Government Committee member, and a Military Affairs Committee member, he bears a major responsibility to the country and the people. Since the 9/18 and 1/28 incidents occurred and continue to this day, he has long been determined to resist Japan and save the country. Mr. Feng is currently in Zhangjiakou, and I also met with him in Zhangjiakou. It has now been decided that he will come to Beijing, but the date of departure is undecided, but it should not be far off. At this moment, he has specially appointed Huang Shaogu as his representative to accompany me to Beijing to inform the Central Government of various opinions. As for what task and title the Central Government will give Mr. Feng, this matter is being carefully considered by the Central Government and has not yet been concretely decided. Mr. Feng himself has no demands or conditions. However, the Central Government must give him a practical and appropriate task and title so that Mr. Feng can do his best to serve the country. This is a matter of fact. In my opinion, since Mr. Feng is determined to resist Japan, the Central Government should give him the task of resisting Japan so that Mr. Feng can be happy to accept it, and the Central Government can also achieve twice the result with half the effort. As for the recent situation in North China, in my observation, Japan is determined to take Rehe. The situation in North China is becoming increasingly urgent, but the military and civilians, both high and low, are determined to resist. This is a good phenomenon. There are two points that prove the psychology of national self-determination: (1) The army is united in heart and mind, waiting only for the order to move out and can depart at any time without any hesitation. (2) Although military pay is insufficient, there are many donations from all sides to aid and support the country. Even officers of all ranks are willing to empty their pockets and contribute their private savings to cover expenses, with no instance of loving money and forgetting the country. When I was in Beiping, I met with many important generals in North China, and I also made detailed inquiries among the people. From Zhang Hanqing to peddlers, all hold the determination to rather be a shattered jade than a whole tile.] Mr. Wang also stated that since Huang Shaogu represents Mr. Feng, he will first go to Gan to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to convey Mr. Feng's intentions.

Changshu

Suzhou-Changshu Road Construction Completed 104

The Suzhou-Changshu Road in this area was ordered to be built by the Construction Department in mid-March of last year, with the Construction Bureau of this area and Wu County jointly undertaking the construction. Work began immediately, starting with the construction of bridges. Currently, the bridges in the Changshu section have been completed. The entire road is approximately ninety li long, with this area responsible for fifty li, including the construction of twenty-seven bridges, the largest of which is twenty-eight meters long, and the smallest fifteen meters. However, the road surface has not yet been paved, so it is not yet open to traffic. Because the Construction Bureau will be ordered to merge, they rushed to complete the roadbed earthworks and culverts. Yesterday, Director Gu telegraphed the county government, requesting that it be forwarded to the Construction Department for the rapid dispatch of personnel to Changshu for acceptance and inspection.

Wuxi

Relief Committee's Surplus Funds Used for Grain Storage Expenses 105

The Grain Management Committee of this area held a committee meeting yesterday in the county government conference room. Li Tiping, Feng Junyan, Zhao Zixin, Wang Li, Chen Zhanru, and others attended, chaired by Chen Chuande. Matters discussed included: (1) This county previously planned to collect five cents per mu for grain storage expenses, but it was ordered to be reviewed and it conflicted with the one-hundredth limit. Another method of raising funds was suggested. Please immediately consider and draft a proposal for approval. (2) A letter from the fifth section of the Civil Affairs Department, transferred by the county government, contained an electric message from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, ordering each province to report the details of grain storage by the end of January for dispatching personnel to check. The above two cases were discussed together. It was resolved that, upon examination, the suggested method of raising funds involved complex procedures and was difficult to implement. A letter was still sent to the county government, requesting that the original proposal to continue collecting grain storage expenses per mu be approved. Before approval is received, in order to cope with emergencies, the committee sent a letter to the County Funds Property Office, requesting that the surplus funds from the flood relief committee last year, which were raised to repair dikes, be reallocated from the relief funds for each district, totaling more than 26,000 yuan, to be collected in full as soon as possible. It also requested the county government to withdraw four-tenths of the two-five treasury bond items from each district and allocate them to grain storage expenses. After the funds are received, grain will be purchased and stored immediately.

Luo Wengan Came to Shanghai Yesterday to Visit Song 106

A joyous banquet was held at the Song residence last night to discuss important matters

Luo Talks about the Sino-Dutch Boxer Indemnity Negotiations in Progress

Agreement to Extend the Special District Court for Three Years

Song Returned to Beijing Last Night, Luo Returns Today

Foreign Minister Luo Wengan arrived in Shanghai by train from Beijing at 5:50 PM yesterday. Yu Ming, Director of the Foreign Ministry's Shanghai Office, and Section Chief Zhao Zhang and others personally welcomed him at the station. Mr. Luo alighted from the train and went directly to the Song residence on Qiqi Road to meet with Acting Executive Yuan President Song Ziwen to inquire about diplomatic matters, financial matters, and dined at the Song residence, talking at length until after 10:00 PM, when Luo took his leave and returned to his residence to rest. This newspaper's reporter visited Mr. Luo last night to inquire about recent diplomatic issues. Mr. Luo's remarks are divided as follows:

Coming to Shanghai to Visit Song 107

Mr. Luo first stated that his visit to Shanghai was solely to meet with Acting Executive Yuan President Song Ziwen to discuss important matters. Since Mr. Song has been delayed in Shanghai due to illness for two weeks without meeting, he had no choice but to come in person to report everything. However, the political affairs in Nanjing are also complex and numerous, and it is inconvenient to stay in Shanghai for a long time, so he plans to return to the capital tomorrow (today).

Mr. Luo also stated that regarding the League of Nations, our chief representative, Dr. Yan Huiqing, has been reporting to the Foreign Ministry via telegram at any time. Dr. Yan will depart for Moscow to assume his post as Ambassador to Russia after the meeting closes. Dutch Boxer Indemnity Negotiations 109

He replied that regarding the Sino-Dutch Boxer Indemnity issue, negotiations have been held repeatedly in Beijing. The country advocates that the use of the returned indemnity should be entirely used for water conservancy projects in Nanjing, such as dredging the Huai River. Joint Declaration of Ma Xiangbo and Zhang Taiyan 115

Using history and anecdotes to prove that the Three Eastern Provinces belong to China

Zhang Taiyan, a master of Chinese classical studies, and Ma Xiangbo, a 94-year-old elder, in view of the League of Nations conference not having reached a resolution on denying the "Manchukuo" state, specifically from the standpoint of Chinese scholars, use historical and anecdotal evidence to prove that the Three Eastern Provinces belong to China. The joint declaration, the full text of which is found below, (it is heard that it will be telegraphed to Geneva to Chief Representative Hui Qing to ask him to announce it to the world):

The Three Eastern Provinces are called Manchuria, but this is only a common name, not the proper name. Manchuria is only a kind of tribe, not the whole of the Three Eastern Provinces. Speaking of ancient history, during the Han Dynasty there already existed Liaodong (now Jinzhou) and Xuantu (now the Eastern Border Region), and in the Ming Dynasty, the Liaodong Regional Military Commission was established, stationed in Shenyang. These were originally inland territories of China, not like vassal states. Considering today's population, there are more than 20 million Han Chinese in the Three Eastern Provinces, and only more than 1 million Manchus. If we talk about national self-determination, the three provinces should belong to the Han people, not to the Manchus. Although the Liao, Jin, and Yuan dynasties entered and ruled China, and Emperor Kangxi of the Qing Dynasty signed the Treaty of Nerchinsk with Russia, (among which one kind was in Latin, all recognized as Chinese land), and their ethnicity has long been assimilated with China. It is still remembered that during the Xianfeng era, Western historians recorded that there were special deer in Chinese Sakhalin Island used to pull carts and cultivate land. Until the Tongzhi era, the island still presented sable pelts, etc. There is no doubt that the Three Eastern Provinces belong to China. Japan's attack on the Three Eastern Provinces clearly knew that the taking was not rightful, so they evaded the charge, calling it self-defense. This was also unacceptable, so they embellished the crime and created the "Manchukuo" state. The people did not submit, and thus there were the Volunteer Armies. Is this not plainly a fabrication?

It is reported that this action, being a joint declaration to the outside world by first-class Chinese scholars, will be able to represent their thousands of disciples, famous professors, scientists, and people in education who are currently serving, to make a public announcement to the world in support of China's inherent sovereignty, proving that the Three Eastern Provinces should belong to China. It is hoped that all compatriots in the country will rise up to save themselves.

Ge Jing'en Comes to Shanghai to Discuss Air Defense Policy 116

All Sectors Respond to Saving the Nation Through Aviation

Ge Jing'en, Director of the Aviation Administration, because all sectors are very enthusiastic about the movement to save the nation through aviation, in order to plan for aviation construction by civil aviation organizations and aviation authorities, and to have unified steps, specially left Hangzhou the day before yesterday (the 8th) at around 9 a.m. He arrived in Shanghai at 2 p.m. and immediately drove to Mayor Wu's residence to discuss matters in detail with Mr. Wu. Lin Xijiang, executive director of the China Aviation Association, had already been waiting at the Wu residence. After a while, he visited the executive directors of the Aviation Association, Wang Zhengting, Wang Xiaolai, Shi Liangcai, Lin Kanghou, and others, and also met with the former Director of the Aviation Administration, Zhang Huichang, to discuss the construction policy of aviation national defense. Yesterday morning, the executive directors of the Aviation Association again talked with Mr. Ge, and also met with the former Director of the Aviation Administration, Huang Bingheng, for detailed discussions. He took a car back to Hangzhou at about 3 p.m. Before leaving, he told reporters briefly that before the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95, the tonnage of our country's navy was ranked fourth in the world. It was not that we didn't work hard on construction, but because there was no meticulous plan and we expanded blindly, so the entire army was wiped out in the Sino-Japanese War of 1894-95. Today, in building the air force, we must learn from the mistakes of the navy, and there must be a meticulous plan in advance. This time, I met with the two former Directors, Zhang and Huang. Both of them are aviation experts, and they gave sincere advice on the choices of the aviation construction policy, which was very beneficial. He discussed with the directors of the Aviation Association the policy of the government and the people working together, so that the government and people's organizations can understand each other, and the facilities will naturally tend to be consistent. The future of aviation construction is very promising. The result of my trip was very good.

Absolute Freedom to Transfer National Troops within Our Territory 119

Japanese Representative Lodges Unreasonable Protest with City Government Yesterday

Our Representative Has Refuted Sternly Based on the Ceasefire Agreement

China Internal News Agency reports that the Japanese representative of the Joint Committee, Consul General Ishii, and Naval Lieutenant Commander Kakuda, visited the Shanghai Municipal Government at 11 a.m. yesterday to see the representative of our side, Secretary General of the Municipal Government Yu Hongjun. Regarding the passage of Chinese troops through Shanghai on the evening of the 7th, they considered it to be a violation of the ceasefire agreement of May 5, 1932, specifically questioned it, and lodged a protest. Secretary General Yu answered that Article 3 of the ceasefire agreement stipulates, "Before a method for the normal recovery of Chinese troops in the area involved in this agreement has been decided, the troops will remain in their current positions." However, the Chinese troops referred to in this agreement refer only to the Chinese troops fighting the Japanese army at that time. When the Japanese army withdrew, this provision was made to avoid conflicts. Therefore, the so-called "Chinese troops" in this agreement cannot include other Chinese troops, otherwise all Chinese troops will be bound by this agreement, which is unreasonable. The Japanese interpretation is neither legal nor reasonable. In short, the Chinese government has absolute freedom and sovereignty to transfer troops within Chinese territory and is not subject to interference from any party. Therefore, China not only considers the troop movements on the 7th not to be a violation of the agreement, but also considers them to be unrelated to the agreement. Firstly, even if we take a step back and acknowledge the Japanese representative's interpretation of Article 2 of the ceasefire agreement (but it is impossible to acknowledge it in fact or in theory), this clause can only be applied before the normal state of the area involved in the agreement has been restored. Now the normal state of the area has long been restored, and it is of course not applicable. Secondly, the Japanese side has repeatedly expressed its desire to restore Sino-Japanese relations. It is regrettable that they are now taking this attitude. They should consider it. At this point, Ishii argued slightly, but ultimately ran out of words, agreed to reconsider, and left.

Initially, When Abandoning Taels and Adopting Yuan, Taels and Yuan Will Be Temporarily Allowed to Be Used Together 120

Regulate Exchange Rate, Silver Taels Will Be Abolished When They Are Used Up

Those Holding Silver Taels Can Freely Request to Mint New Coins

Regarding the issue of abandoning taels and adopting yuan, the Ministry of Finance has decided to implement it on March 1. The money industry will also be changed to the yuan standard at the same time. In the initial implementation, silver yuan and silver taels will be used together. The details are recorded as follows:

Weight and Fineness of New Currency 121

Yesterday, a reporter from the New Voice News Agency met with leaders in the banking industry. According to them, after the Ministry of Finance decided to abandon taels and adopt yuan, the weight of the currency will be 16.6971 grams (equivalent to 7 mace and 2 candareens of Kuping taels), and the fineness will be 88, with 23.493448 grams of pure silver (equivalent to 6 mace, 3 candareens, and 1 li of Kuping taels).

Taels and Yuan Temporarily Allowed to Be Used Together 122

When abandoning taels and adopting yuan, in the initial implementation, in order to take into account the difficulties in converting silver taels into silver yuan for various industries, the Ministry of Finance has specifically stipulated that the legal silver yuan price is 7 mace and 1.5 candareens, and the silver tael price is 1 yuan and 4 jiao. In the initial implementation, silver yuan and taels will be allowed to be used together until the silver taels are used up.

Silver Tael Notes Will Stop Being Exchanged 123

Among the Chinese banks, those issuing silver tael banknotes are now only the Bank of Communications. Among the foreign banks are the Hongkong and Shanghai Banking Corporation, the Chartered Bank, etc. After the abandonment of taels is implemented, the banknotes issued will be canceled. Regarding the implementation of silver tael clearing and silver tael remittances by the bank clearing house, it is heard that it will be submitted to the committee for discussion and cessation.

Permission for Free Minting 124

After receiving orders from the Ministry, the Central Mint will immediately start minting new coins, and free minting will be allowed. According to the Third Article of the People's Republic Ordinance, pure silver is 6 mace and 4.8 candareens, 23.9775048 grams, and the fineness is 89, but it has not been minted. The Sun Yat-sen coins and Yuan Shikai coins currently circulating in the country have been minted to an amount of over 300 million yuan.

Cai Yuanpei's Remarks 125

The League for the Protection of Civil Rights Cannot Be Called Illegal

Since Madam Sun Yat-sen, Soong Ching-ling, and Cai Yuanpei, among others, initiated the organization of the China League for Civil Rights, the people of the country have been very sympathetic to this organization. However, when the Peiping branch of the League was established on the 30th of last month, the Peiping Municipal Party Department sent letters to the Municipal Government, etc., considering it an illegal organization and asking them not to accept any requests from the League. Yesterday, regarding this matter, the reporter specifically visited Cai Yuanpei, vice chairman of the League, at the Academia Sinica to inquire about his attitude towards this matter. According to him, the organization of this League is based on the rights given to the people by the Provisional Constitution. The purpose of the organization of this League is to protect human rights and promote the rule of law. Its purpose is pure and its attitude is open and aboveboard. It absolutely cannot be called "illegal." On the contrary, all opposition to the League's claims is "illegal." Furthermore, in terms of facts, when the Peiping Municipal Party Department sent a letter to the Municipal Government, denying the establishment of the Peiping branch of the League (January 31), the League had already received an official letter from the Peiping Municipal Government regarding the rescue of anti-Japanese youths in Peiping. This shows that the League has already been recognized as a proper and legitimate organization in fact.

Mr. Yang Xingfo was also present. Mr. Yang also said that the previous news reports about his speech, saying that the "Anti-Imperialist League" would send representatives to the Far East to investigate the Manchurian Incident, was actually a mistake for the "World Anti-War Conference" and should be corrected. The conference is organized by scholars from all over the world and will investigate the Manchurian Incident from a position of justice and fairness.

"Respected Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Communications in Nanjing, according to a letter from the Peiping Postal Workers' Union, the Peiping Postmaster Ba Lidi colluded with military police on January 2 to detain 12 executive committee members of the Union's Anti-Japanese Association. They have not been brought before the court or released. Since postal workers are also citizens, how can they be guilty of resisting Japan? Human rights are clearly recorded in the law, and arbitrary trampling is especially inappropriate. It is hoped that the Peiping authorities will be immediately ordered to release the detained postal workers and that Postmaster Ba Lidi, who abused his power, will be punished to uphold civil rights. Chairman Song Qingling and Cai Yuanpei of the China League for the Protection of Civil Rights."

Collision Between Two Jiangnan Vessels 129

"Ningbo" and "Taiping" Vessels Collide Head-On

Ten or More Sha Ships and Civilian Vessels Suffer

Many Boatmen and Passengers Drowned

At about 12:00 noon yesterday, the "Ningbo" steamship of the Taikoo Company, after leaving the Yitaixing Wharf in Dongjiadu, Pudong, after unloading coal, suddenly collided head-on with the "Taiping" steamship. The "Taiping" vessel immediately reversed, then moved forward again, intending to stop the vessel, but unexpectedly damaged six sand ships moored along the Pudong waterfront, and sank two rowing boats, one yellow vegetable boat, and one sailing vessel. The number of boatmen and passengers drowned is estimated to be more than thirty. The results of the investigation are recorded below.

Circumstances of the Accident 130

South of Dongjiadu, south of the Pudong waterfront, in addition to various civilian vessels usually moored, there are also various sand ships, numbering several hundred, divided into rows of seven or eight, moored in sequence. At about 12:00 noon yesterday, the "Ningbo" steamship, after unloading the coal it transported at the Yitaixing Coal Depot in Pudong, raised anchor and sailed north. At that time, the "Taiping" steamship was speeding south, intending to turn around there to enter and moor at the wharf. The two vessels collided head-on with slight carelessness. But hearing a loud bang, after the bows of the two vessels came into contact, the bow of the "Ningbo" vessel skewed towards Pudong. The "Taiping" vessel turned and sped diagonally towards Puxi. The engineers on the "Taiping" urgently reversed, but then went forward again, wanting to correct the vessel's position before proceeding. Unexpectedly, the bow of the vessel skewed directly towards the Puxi side, and collided with the Shandong sand ships moored there. After the sand ships were hit, they shifted to the side. Several other sand ships parked next to them, unable to withstand the pressure, all shifted backwards. The row of sand ships behind, having been squeezed by the sand ships in front, also fell back along with the force. They fell in sequence until they stopped at the Santae Wharf. Among them, the sand ships that were hit and damaged on the bow, stern, and body due to the pressure numbered six in total. About a dozen others were slightly damaged. There were also two rowing boats, one yellow vegetable boat, and one sailing vessel, all crushed by the sand ships.

Capsizing Vessels and Injuring People 131

At the time, because the rowing boats and other vessels were small, they were unable to save the sand ships, resulting in them all being crushed and sinking to the bottom of the river. When the rowing boats capsized, the passengers and boatmen on board, numbering more than fifty, all drowned with the vessels. Seeing this, neighboring vessels rushed forward to try to rescue them. The water patrol team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, hearing the alarm, also dispatched police officers Jiang Bin, Zhang Kefeng, and others to make efforts to rescue them. As a result, only a dozen boatmen were rescued. More than thirty others could not be rescued and drowned tragically. Their bodies floated away without a trace. According to statistics, the losses suffered by each vessel were numerous. Among them, the most severely affected was the sailing vessel. The sailing vessel was moored near the Laiyi Wharf and had loaded more than twenty passengers yesterday, setting sail at about 12:00 noon. At that time, it happened to encounter the sand ship squeeze, resulting in it being immediately hit and overturned. All the passengers on board fell into the water. Only five or six people were rescued on the spot. Among them, Sun Guanxi, although rescued, suffered serious injuries. He was sent to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment, and it is said that his life may be in danger. After the two rowing boats sank, only one boatman was rescued. After the yellow vegetable boat sank, everyone on board drowned completely, without a single survivor. As for the sand ships, Yang Hua Da's vessel had a giant hole smashed into its stern, with a diameter of over two feet. Yang Junchen's vessel had a huge hole smashed into its waist, and water quickly entered the bottom of the vessel. Six or seven other vessels of unknown names had their bows and sterns smashed in to varying degrees.

Aftermath 132

After the incident, the "Ningbo" steamship of the Taikoo Company, although it collided with the "Taiping" steamship, its bow was not damaged, so it continued to sail north. The bow of the "Taiping" vessel was damaged, so it sailed to the Pudong China Wharf to moor for repairs. However, more than twenty boatmen and others who sank to the bottom of the river had not yet surfaced as of 7:00 p.m. It was only heard that a drowned corpse, already divided into two sections, had been recovered from the Pudong waterfront near the South Wharf. It was indeed tragic.

The Special District Court Tries Hard to Improve 133

The Central News Agency reports that the Shanghai Special District Court Agreement expires on April 1. Regarding the issue of modification after the expiration, the British Ambassador Lampson and the Dutch Minister Dr. Beelaerts van Blokland have exchanged views with Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Xu Mo in Beijing. As for the inability to immediately enforce civil judgments, this was a matter from last spring, and we have been working hard to improve. Since the appointment of President Shen Jiaxuan, we have been working hard to find ways to reform in order to satisfy all parties.

Disputes Over Water Fee Issues: Water Company Proposes Alternative Solution 134

Real Estate Association Requests Three Items, Ningbo Compatriot Association Sends Letter Requesting Negotiation

The National News Agency reports that the Shanghai Waterworks Company, a British company, has changed its water meters, and the water fees have exceeded the previous price by seven or eight times. The Real Estate Association has therefore resolved to refuse to pay unanimously, and the company has implemented water cuts, causing conflicts with users. The reporter visited both sides yesterday and learned that the company has proposed an alternative solution. The details are recorded below.

Real Estate Association Says Water Fee Exceeds Rent 135

According to Dou Yaoting, a representative of the Real Estate Association, who spoke to reporters, the water company has always charged water fees according to 6% of the rent, that is, a rent of 100 yuan, a water price of 6 yuan. Later, the water company stipulated that shareholders' interest should be at least 9%, so it was not enough to cover expenses, and it was increased to 7.5% of the rent, charging 7.5 yuan per 100 yuan. Both sides were at peace until June of last year, when the water company suddenly used the excuse that users were overly wasteful, and with the approval of the Public Works Department, changed to installing water meters and charging 6 jiao and 2.5 fen per 1,000 gallons. But after this change, water fees for large mansions and buildings were reduced compared to before (because large mansions have fewer people and use less water), while water fees for commoner residences increased greatly. Especially in places where factories were gathered, even for each building, the rent was only 30 yuan, while the water price was more than 40 yuan. In this way, the landlords not only had no rent, but had to subsidize some. Although the building had twenty or more households, if each person used 10 gallons of water per day, the total monthly amount would be more than 7,000 gallons, and the fee would be quite large. Therefore, the landlords could only unanimously refuse to pay.

Stop Water Cuts, Propose Three Requirements 136

Now the water company, disregarding people's lives, is implementing water cuts, and the conflict that occurred the day before yesterday was expected. If it is not resolved, it is inevitable that other more unfortunate incidents will occur. The Real Estate Association has appointed me (Dou himself) as a representative to visit Jones, director of the Public Works Department, to promptly stop this illegal action of the water company. However, yesterday's newspaper reported that I had met with Jones the day before yesterday and talked for half an hour, which is inaccurate. I only had one discussion with the chairman of the Western Property Owners Association. Yesterday afternoon, I went to the Public Works Department with the chairman of the Western Property Owners Association to meet with Jones. First, I requested that the water company no longer continue water cuts to maintain people's lives, and proposed three requirements: (1) It would be best if the previous charge of 7.5% of the rent could be restored; (2) Otherwise, install a water meter for each user (now only one general meter is installed per lane), and the water fee will be borne by the tenants, and the landlord is willing to reduce the rent; (3) Even if the tenants bear the cost, the water company should also reduce the water price to sympathize with the lives of commoners. Later, Jones agreed to discuss it at the Public Utilities Committee before leaving.

The Company Expresses Its Difficulties and Has Proposed an Alternative Solution 137

The reporter then visited the water company to inquire about everything. A Westerner from the company's business section came out and said that the company installed water meters in accordance with the instructions of the Public Works Department and spent more than 1 million yuan on purchasing these water meters. The reason for the water cuts was that since last June, after the company changed to charging according to the water meter system, the fees for large mansions and buildings were less than before, and real estate companies paid happily. Water fees for commoner residences increased, and the Real Estate Association resolved to refuse to pay unanimously. For more than half a year, not a penny has been collected. If this continues, the company will not be able to maintain it, so it has to take the method of water cuts as a response. But the company also knows that the water price is too high, even more than the rent, and a remedy must be sought. Therefore, the company has now proposed an alternative solution, that is, to base the standard of water price on the level of rent. Assuming the rent is more than 100 yuan, the water fee is 6 jiao per 1,000 gallons, and if it is less than 50 yuan, it is only 3 jiao. But the detailed prices have not yet been determined. The program has been submitted to the Public Works Department to be forwarded to the Real Estate Association. If it can be allowed, other details will be discussed again.

Ningbo Compatriot Association Asks to Open Water Pipes in Ningbo Lane 138

The National News Agency reports that the Ningbo Native Place Association of Shanghai, due to the fact that the drinking water needed every day was cut off by the Waterworks Company on the 3rd of this month, the chairman of the Association, Yu Qiaqing, sent a letter to the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association, asking them to negotiate with the Bureau of Works to open the water pipes, etc. The Association immediately forwarded a letter to the Bureau of Works: "To the honorable ones, we are writing to you as per a letter received from Mr. Yu Qiaqing, chairman of the Ningbo Native Place Association of Shanghai: Since the Shanghai Waterworks Company installed water meters, the water fees have been more than doubled compared to before, and therefore the water fees have not been paid to this day. We already sent a letter to your Association on August 5, protesting to the Bureau of Works to reduce the water fees. Half a year has passed and it has not been resolved, and the Waterworks Company has not collected the water fees from our Association. Unexpectedly, on the 3rd of this month, the Waterworks Company suddenly closed the drinking water supply to Ningbo Lane on Lloyd Road, causing panic among the residents. We are writing to ask your Association to quickly negotiate with the Bureau of Works to resolve this issue as soon as possible, reduce the water fees, and formally open the drinking water supply to Ningbo Lane on Lloyd Road to maintain the livelihood of the people.

Upon investigation, everyone knows that people cannot live without water and fire, and that the purpose of water meters is to control waste. The current method of installation only increases the revenue of the water company, which is not in line with the purpose. The water company is not planning on controlling waste and not increasing fees, but instead is cutting off the water to achieve its arbitrary claims, and does not value, or perhaps does not know, the relationship between water and human life. Our Association is extremely worried about public safety. For the reasons stated in the letter above, we are writing to ask your Bureau to quickly order the Waterworks Company to formally turn on the water to maintain people's lives and await a resolution.

And to the Ningbo Native Place Association of Shanghai: We are replying to your letter of February 4 regarding the Waterworks Company's illegal water cut. Upon investigation, water is indispensable to people's daily life, and it hinders both life and fire safety. It seems that the emergency self-defense method that the law does not permit can be adopted. Apart from writing to the Bureau of Works to order the Waterworks Company to formally turn on the water to await a resolution, we are replying accordingly. Please investigate."

National Goods Manufacturers Strictly Guard Against Cunning and Deception 139

Please Note Proof from Two National Goods Organizations

Zhanghua Woolen Mill, Yifeng Enamel Factory, Nanchang Copper Factory, Yaguang Manufacturing Company, Dachina Match Company, Tianchu MSG Factory, Xiaofang Photographic Paper Factory, Zhaofeng French Factory, Guohua Chemical Industry, Zhonghua French Factory, Dafeng Industrial Factory, Huafu Hat Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Ruihe Brick and Tile Factory, Kangcheng Liquor Factory, China Iron Factory, Huayang Dyeing and Weaving Factory, Dafeng Raw Material Factory, Huaguo Glass Factory, Shanghai Organ Factory, China Chemical Industry, Dacheng Weaving Factory, Dahua Iron Factory, Ruihe Crucible Factory, and forty-five other national goods factories, jointly sent a letter yesterday to the China National Products Maintenance Association and the Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, emphasizing merchants who sell goods and requesting proof of national goods. The original letter stated, (part omitted above) Our national goods factories each have a fixed registered trademark, but merchants often like to create their own trademarks and order various goods from national goods factories. There are many types of these trademarks, with no standards at all. Moreover, merchants prioritize profit. Today, they order goods from national goods factories, but if they cannot satisfy their desire for profit due to the cost of raw materials, it is difficult to guarantee that they will not order the same kind of goods from foreign factories tomorrow. Because they first ordered from national goods factories, they also promote their products as national goods. When they later order from foreign factories due to various reasons, they still pretend to sell national goods. This kind of deceptive tactic is seen and heard from time to time, and it is difficult for outsiders to detect. In order to prevent this from happening, the government requires customs to investigate national goods factories every six months to clarify whether the trademarks used are their own products. This method is well-intentioned and thorough. However, it does not treat goods with trademarks created by merchants the same as the national goods factories' own products. Therefore, fearing that these merchants will seek proof from national goods organizations to promote their products, we have jointly stated the contents and sent a letter to your association, requesting that you refuse to provide proof for such goods to avoid being exploited and to protect the interests of national goods factories' own products (part omitted below).

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Program for Promoting National Goods 140

The First and Second Phases are the Implementation Period for the Members Themselves, and the Third Phase is the Expanded Implementation Period

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce issued a notice yesterday, stating, "To Whom It May Concern: The Fourth National Products Promotion Committee of this Chamber discussed the 'Program for Promoting National Products' drafted by Committee Members Wang and Xu and submitted it for public resolution. The original proposed measures included: The first phase is six months, the implementation period for the committee members themselves: (A) Committee members and branch committee members should reduce or eliminate daily necessities related to personal clothing, food, and daily activities, such as decorations and extravagant expenses. Otherwise, for other types of necessities, if national goods can be substituted, they should first be promoted and practiced as an example. (B) At the same time, each branch should conduct a thorough investigation of the national goods and non-national goods components of each industry within these six months, and report to this Chamber. (C) Sales businesses must uniformly mark national goods and non-national goods when selling goods to attract the attention of consumers and make it easy to identify. (D) This Chamber or its branches should organize propaganda sessions and national goods weeks in their affiliated factories, businesses, and organizations to give regular lectures. The second phase is six months, the implementation period for the members' affiliated factories and businesses: (A) Manufacturing industries must substitute national goods for anything that does not harm the quality of the manufactured products. (B) The businesses and shops affiliated with the sales industry should designate one day each week to sell national goods exclusively. The third phase has no fixed time period and is the expanded implementation period. If there are no national goods to substitute for the raw materials and machinery of the manufacturing industry, each industry should find its own way to research and manufacture them. If the strength is insufficient, it should be reported to this Chamber to request joint assistance from each industry. Within a possible scope and a reasonable period, it is necessary to gradually provide domestic products in order to achieve the goal of complete national goods. Secondly, (A) Production aspects are divided into one program: First step: research and reward the export of existing national products; second step: research the manufacturing methods of foreign goods and actively imitate them; third step: research the semi-finished products of imported raw materials. (B) Consumption aspects are divided into two programs: First, request the government to issue a clear order to encourage government agencies, schools, the military, and the public to use national goods and punish them for using foreign goods. Second, request various social groups to encourage ladies from all walks of life to take pride in using national goods and feel ashamed of using foreign goods," etc. The above were discussed and passed, and separate letters were sent to the branch associations of each industry for reference and implementation. In addition to sending separate letters, we are correspondingly recording the case and sending this letter to your association for your review and careful handling.

Ma Yubao Passed Away in Shanghai Due to Illness 141

A Central News Agency report stated that Ma Yubao, former military advisor to the National Government and former military governor of Jiangxi Province, whose courtesy name was Yuanliang, passed away at the Red Cross Hospital on Haig Road on the day before yesterday at Maoshi (5-7 AM) due to illness. Mr. Ma was very friendly with Chairman Lin of the National Government and Mayor Wu of this city. They were colleagues who shared hardships during the revolution and were among the first soldiers to respond to the Wuchang Uprising. He was also the first person appointed as military governor by the Premier when he took office as the provisional president. He was honest, simple, and sincere, and truly a revolutionary hero. When Mayor Wu heard the news, he was extremely saddened and has telegraphed the central government and sent personnel to handle the funeral arrangements. The remains have now been sent to the China Funeral Home, and the coffin will be sealed at 11:00 AM on the 11th.

Labor and Management Should Sincerely Cooperate During National Crisis 142

The General Labor Union Specially Sends a Letter to the Chamber of Commerce to Eliminate Disputes and Save the Nation Together

The City General Labor Union believes that labor-management disputes in various industries are greatly hindering the development of industry and affecting social order. Therefore, based on the resolutions of the Second Congress of Representatives, it sent a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting it to notify all factories and businesses not to close factories or dismiss workers on the pretext of the national crisis. At the same time, it also ordered all labor unions to uphold the spirit of labor-management cooperation and instruct all workers to step up production. Therefore, serious disputes have been caused more than once. If they are not corrected, they will harm the lives of workers and affect social order. In view of the foregoing, in addition to ordering all labor unions to instruct all workers to work hard and increase production in the spirit of labor-management cooperation during this national crisis, we are correspondingly sending a letter to your association to notify all members to implement and cooperate sincerely to eliminate disputes and save the nation. This is our sincere hope. To the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai General Labor Union."

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Announces That Delivery Personnel Should Carry Delivery Slips 143

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday notified the three sub-offices, the 197 trade associations, and the 22 store members: "Regarding the matter of notification, it has been found that merchants often fail to attach delivery slips to goods delivered to customers due to temporary oversight. This leads to local detectives mistaking them for peddlers and detaining them, which is no small matter as it affects business reputation. In order to ensure commercial safety, this Chamber has specially issued this notification. We hope that all members will, when transporting goods in the future, clearly indicate the quantity of goods and the names and addresses of the recipients on the delivery slip and carry it with the goods to avoid unnecessary complications. This is of utmost importance."

Yu Yan Discusses the Reorganization of Railway Operations (Continued) 149

丨Contributing Two Points for Future Direction丨

(II) Streamlining Passenger Transportation (A) Regarding the use of trains by personnel from various agencies, in the past, they could arbitrarily keep accounts, which was chaotic. I immediately worked with the chief accountant to draft six reorganization measures, which were submitted to the academy for approval and filed, and distributed to various railways for implementation to eliminate abuses. (B) Ordering measures for academic groups to travel by train. In the past, there was no fixed standard for preferential treatment for academic groups to travel by train, and there were many abuses. Nine measures have been revised, stipulating that they must be statutory academic groups and submitted by the Ministry of Education or the provincial and municipal governments to this Ministry for processing, and restrictions have been added to prevent abuses. (C) Reorganizing free tickets and the cleanliness and heating of passenger car equipment. Orders have been issued to strictly limit the daredevilry of free tickets on various railways. As for the precautions for passenger cars and the service of on-board staff, orders have been issued to various railways for compliance at any time. (III) Reorganizing Military Transportation. For matters such as military relief and public goods transportation, the railways were almost regarded as doing errands. This concept is fundamentally wrong. Railway transportation has original costs and is of a commercial nature. The prosperity or decline of business is of utmost importance to the future of the railways and the income of the country. Regarding military transportation, in the past, all accounts were kept.

This has been specially noted when implementing military transport regulations and handling them strictly. In the past six months, there have been no less than hundreds of cases where various parties arbitrarily requested transportation and were rationally rejected by this Ministry. Because the original military transport regulations were already very generous, it was inappropriate to accommodate them arbitrarily. (IV) Rectifying Disaster Relief Transportation. The loss of freight costs for various railways regarding disaster relief transportation reaches more than two million yuan each year. There have been rumors that the disaster relief transportation itself is not true or complete, so reorganization is inevitable. Since Yan took office, strict handling has been ordered. The free transportation of relief goods has been submitted to the academy for cancellation, and the flat-rate price reduction measures for rice and grain have also been stopped. (V) Restricting Public Transportation. The charging method for public special materials has been used for a long time, and many parties have exceeded the scope of requests for transportation, which is inevitably chaotic. An explanation has been added, and an order has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for filing, limiting it only to the central and local directly affiliated agencies and the articles needed for office use, which can be transported at half price in cash. Many parties have been rejected for their requests for transportation based on this. (VI) Developing Freight Transportation (A) The running time of freight cars on various railways is mostly uncertain, which goes against the spirit of scientific management. Orders have been issued to various railways to improve this immediately, open regular freight cars every day, and run mixed trains every day, and facilitate the transportation of fresh goods, and limit large packages to promote business. (B) The railway package business is closely related to the postal parcel business, and the number of postal parcels transported is of great importance to the package income of various railways. In 1921, the loss of freight costs for various railways transporting postal parcels reached more than 26 million. This postal parcel was originally a railway business itself. The post office used a special low freight rate, so the railway had no way to compete. The losses suffered have been calculated by statistical methods and submitted to the Ministry of Transportation for consideration of adding postal parcel freight costs, and efforts have been made to improve the package transportation of various railways to compete. (To be continued)

British Aviation New Record Speed, Height, and Distance 150

The Effectiveness of Shell Aviation Gasoline

Those who care about the progress of aviation know that Britain has broken three world records for speed, height, and non-stop long-distance flight. The speed record was broken in September 1931 at Calshot at a rate of 407.5 miles per hour. The height record was broken in September 1932 at Bristol at a height of 43,976 feet. The non-stop long-distance flight record was broken from February 6 to 8 this year from Cranwell to South Africa, covering a total distance of 5,340 miles. When the world height record was broken, the pilot used Shell aviation lubricant oil, which contributed to the success. The non-stop long-distance flight was achieved with Shell aviation gasoline.

Red Pills Made Upstairs in a Restaurant 152

Four Men and Women Arrested, Countless Red Pills Seized

Song Bingzheng and Chen Yaoting, Chinese detectives of the Public Concession Anti-Smoking Department, learned that the upstairs of Weishunxing Restaurant, a well-known pork rib restaurant at No. 313-314, opposite the Sanshan Guild Hall on Fuzhou Road, was a red pill manufacturing facility. Therefore, at 2:30 PM on the day before yesterday, they secretly went to search the place with West Detective Park Bobo and Detectives Ye Yusi and Xu Guirong. They arrested four people, including Yin Guoliang, Zhang Xiaodi, Huang Delin, and the woman Yin Wangshi, all from Wuxi. They seized numerous bags of red and white pills, countless red pill manufacturing raw materials, five manufacturing machines, and equipment such as printing and boxing tools, as well as more than 40 yuan in cash. The remaining money, estimated at six or seven thousand yuan, was also taken back to the Laozha Gate Police Station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu prosecuted them in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law, and said that the police had not yet chemically tested the drugs and raw materials seized due to time constraints, so they could not determine their names. He requested the court to postpone the hearing once after interrogation to facilitate chemical testing. Subsequently, Detective Chen submitted a report on the search process. Yin Guoliang had

mutually accused and shirked responsibility. Qian Hongye, the chief of the criminal court, reviewed the report and ordered all defendants to be remanded in custody for another hearing.

Today's Opening of Various Industry Insurance Management Offices 155

Local business leaders Wang Yansong, Fang Jiaobo, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Songyuan, Zhu Wenqi, etc., recognizing the significant importance of the insurance industry to society and individual interests, and that it has been manipulated by foreign merchants for years, with no protection of policyholders' legal rights, have specifically organized Shanghai Various Industries Insurance General Management Office Co., Ltd. on the second floor of the Silk Industry Building at the intersection of Hankou Road and Shilu Road to promote Chinese-owned insurance, regain rights and interests, and safeguard the interests of policyholders by handling procedures. They have elected Wang Yansong as chairman, Chen Songyuan, Zhu Wenqi, and Lu Wenshao as standing directors, Fang Jiaobo as general manager, and Ji Jiaxing and Bao Jingdi as assistant managers. It officially opens today (the 10th) and begins operations on the same day. Its business scope includes: (1) Managing various types of insurance such as life, fire, automobile, and accident; (2) Handling all procedures arising from disasters on behalf of policyholders; (3) Answering inquiries regarding various types of insurance, and researching the manipulation and monopoly of Shanghai residents by foreign insurance companies, which is deeply painful. Now, the company has arisen in response to the times, and its business development can be assured.

Female Abductor Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment 156

Jiang Xiangsheng, owner of Shunxing Iron Shop at 276 North Sea Road, has a daughter named Guilin, who is 29 years old and still unmarried. Her aunt, Xu Jiangshi, harbored intentions of abduction and sale, and repeatedly enticed her with sweet words, saying that if she was willing to run away from her father, she would be chosen a satisfactory husband, with whom she could entrust her life, which would be better than guarding an empty room alone, shadows keeping each other company. The daughter, originally lovesick, agreed with her aunt and conspired. On December 27th, she took gold jewelry and fled with her aunt. The aunt colluded with a woman named Zhu Zhangshi, who resided at 116 MikeGaoLuo Road in the French Concession, and abducted the daughter to Songjiang, selling her to Zhao A'quan's wife, obtaining 50 yuan in silver for the sale. Jiang, after losing his daughter, immediately posted rewards in newspapers seeking her whereabouts. It was not until the 6th of this month that a so-called "Songjiang boss" reported to Jiang. He went to Songjiang to investigate, but Zhao A'quan had already fled. He only brought the daughter back. After questioning her about the details, he rushed to 77 Defen Lane to negotiate with his sister, Xu Jiangshi, and demand the return of the stolen gold jewelry. Xu Jiangshi, in accordance with the date set by her brother Jiang Xiangsheng, went to Zhu Zhangshi's home. While they were arguing, Xu Jiangshi also took the opportunity to escape. She was subsequently discovered by French police, who took everyone to the French Concession police station and transferred them to the Old Gate police station. Yesterday, they were sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Qian interrogated them and sentenced Zhu Zhangshi to two years of imprisonment.

All spaces for writing the names and addresses of the recipient and sender, as well as for affixing stamps, are clearly marked. Type A (made of white paper) sells for 30 cents per hundred, and Type B (yellow) sells for 20 cents in national currency per hundred. A notice has been issued stating that the Shanghai Administration and all its branches and stamp sales offices have them for sale. Using them to send letters is truly convenient.
