Tax Bureau Inquires to Greyhound Racing Association 163

Our government has never collected taxes from the greyhound racing track

The greyhound association claims to have paid stamp duty, to whom did it actually pay?

The greyhound association investigation opened for the third day yesterday

Xie Qijun, Director of the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance, because the Greyhound Racing Association case involves stamp duty, which is currently under the jurisdiction of the department, specially sent a letter to the association. The original text of the letter is as follows: To the Greyhound Racing Association,

It is noted that in the past two days, the British Consular Court has held a hearing on the case of your association suing Martin, the former Deputy Chief of the Public Works Department, and McNaughten, the former Chairman of the Board. Mr. White Ayes, during the court questioning, replied that your association had deducted 11 percent from the prize money of the dog ticket, of which 1 percent was used to pay the Chinese government stamp duty, and stated that this amount was paid secretly as a political event, etc. Now, under government orders, we solemnly request that you clarify to whom the aforementioned tax was actually paid, on what date it was paid, and the number of the check used to pay the money, item by item. Furthermore, the national government has never collected taxes from the greyhound racing track. If your association does not truthfully disclose the aforementioned details, the public will inevitably regard it as extortion. Then, your association and the recipient of the money will certainly bear the responsibility.

Therefore, we specially ask you to investigate and reply. With best wishes,

Xie Qi, February 9th, 22nd year.

The Greyhound Racing Association's lawsuit against Martin, the current acting Extra Chief of the Public Works Department, and McNaughten, the former Chairman of the Board, after the plaintiff's evidence was heard the day before yesterday, the defendant's lawyer, Hoberu, immediately requested the court to dismiss the case, saying that the plaintiff's statements were unfounded and that the defendant had no need to respond. When the trial opened for the third day yesterday morning, Hoberu made a statement on legal points, saying that the plaintiff alleged that the police prevented a member of the Greyhound Association from entering the garden on the night the Ming Garden was ordered to be closed, and that the member referred to was the plaintiff's lawyer, Harris, but the plaintiff has not yet proven that Harris is a member of the association. Now, the defendant has answered all the plaintiff's evidence one by one in the defense, so there is no need to order the defendant to testify in the witness box. Then, he read out Knachten's defense, saying that whether McNaughten was in a private capacity or as a director of the Public Works Department, there were no grounds for prosecution.

Murderer in the Tragic Death of Li Minghui's Lover, Feng Deqian 164

Wang Nengxiang sentenced to life imprisonment

Li Minghui's lover, Feng Deqian, and Zheng Guoyou, in March last year, became enemies in Hong Kong due to a love triangle. Zheng instigated Wang Nengxiang, a carpenter from Tongzhou in Hong Kong, and others to assassinate Feng on the way at night. Afterwards, Zheng was arrested by British officials in the area, interrogated, and found guilty, and sentenced to death. Now, his family is pleading with Hong Kong gentry to beg the British officials to spare Zheng's life, so the execution has been postponed. The murderer, Wang Nengxiang, fled to Shanghai after killing Feng, hiding in the Xiexu Road in Nanshi. He was later arrested by Lu Liankui, the chief detective of the Public Concession Police Department, and handed over to the First Special District Local Court. After obtaining the confession of the accomplice from the British Consular Court in Hong Kong, Li Minghui was summoned, and the court repeatedly held hearings and reached a conclusion. Yesterday morning, when the time for the sentencing arrived, Judge Qian Hongye ascended the seat in the First Criminal Court at 9:00 AM, ordered the defendant Wang Nengxiang to be brought to the court, and after questioning him, immediately announced the verdict: Wang Nengxiang was sentenced to life imprisonment for premeditated murder and deprived of public rights for life. After the verdict, the prisoner was taken by the police back to the police station for detention, awaiting execution after confirmation.

Like a Scene from a Chivalrous Movie: Western Pilot's Benevolent Heart and Chivalrous Spirit 165

Chinese child in Anqing suddenly suffers from rabies

Life cannot be guaranteed if not treated in Shanghai within 24 hours

Western pilot flies to Beijing at risk in dense fog

The child arrived in Shanghai for medical treatment within 24 hours

On the morning of the day before yesterday, the plane of the China National Aviation Corporation from Hanzhong to the east was piloted by Western pilot Norris and Chinese pilot Pang. There were only two passengers in the plane, one was a child named Huisheng, who was only seven years old, and the other was an old woman, who was the child's grandmother. When the plane was less than a few miles away from Hanzhong, the weather suddenly deteriorated, and

The dense fog was extremely thick. 166

Therefore, when the plane arrived at Anqing Airport, Hanzhong Company telegraphed the director of the airport, instructing him to stop the eastward flight to avoid danger. So the child and the old woman stayed at Anqing Airport. About one o'clock in the afternoon, the child suddenly fell ill, and his condition looked like rabies, trying to bite people around him. The grandmother immediately asked the doctor at the airport to diagnose him. The result of the diagnosis was that the child's illness required

Immediate injection in Shanghai. 167

If it exceeded 24 hours, it would be incurable. Then the old woman was very frightened. At that time, Western pilot Mr. Norris saw the situation and felt pity, and resolutely decided to fly the child and the woman to Nanjing, regardless of the difficulties, and decided to take the night train to Shanghai that night, so that they could arrive in Shanghai within 24 hours. After the plan was decided, he mustered his courage and set off,

Advancing in the dense fog. 168

When he arrived in Beijing at 3:00 PM, he immediately telegraphed Dr. Qiaodai, the director of the Seventh Bureau of Health in Shanghai, to report the matter and ask for a solution. And Mr. Norris himself, at 11:00 PM that night, personally accompanied the old woman and the child on the night express train from Beijing to Shanghai. He arrived in Shanghai at about 8:00 AM yesterday morning, and Dr. Qiaodai, the director of the Public Works Department Health Department, had already sent an ambulance to wait at the North Station. When Mr. Norris and others arrived at the station, they immediately took the car and sent the child and the old woman to the Western Isolation Hospital on Bazilu Road, where the hospital doctor gave them treatment. It is said that the situation is still good. Mr. Norris is truly worthy of being a person who sees righteousness and courage.

Detailed Account in Western Newspapers 169

The Da Mei Evening News reported that yesterday (the 8th) a seven-year-old child, Wei Shan, was suspected of being bitten by a rabid dog. Accompanied by his grandmother and doctor Wang, he took a China National Aviation Corporation plane from Hankou to Shanghai for treatment. However, not long after departing from Hankou, he encountered a strong wind and rain. After flying over the wind and rain zone, he encountered dense fog, making the voyage extremely difficult. When he arrived in Anqing at noon, the pilot Norris received a telegram instructing him not to advance any further. Later, at 2:00 PM, the child's condition worsened, and the doctor claimed that only by rushing to Shanghai and injecting rabies serum within 24 hours could there be any hope of rescue. Norris, with a chivalrous heart, was not afraid of danger and obstacles, and then tried to set off at 3:00 PM, hoping to arrive in Beijing in the evening and catch the night train to Shanghai. The journey was extremely difficult. At times, he could only be a few feet away from the river surface, and even had to fly along the water surface. Finally, he was able to reach Nanjing as scheduled, and the child arrived safely in Shanghai this morning, and was notified in advance by Associated Press reporter Mr. Jin in Ning and telegraphed to Qiaodai of the Public Works Department Health Department in this area, who sent an ambulance to meet him at the station and immediately sent him to the Western Isolation Hospital for treatment. It has just been heard that the child's condition has greatly improved, but it is currently undetermined whether he is suffering from a rabid dog bite. The fact that Norris and Pang (transliteration), the pilots of the China National Aviation Corporation, disregarded the strange dangers of wind, rain, and fog, could stop but did not stop, and took saving the child's life as their goal, and were able to arrive in Shanghai on time and save his condition, their benevolent heart and chivalrous spirit is truly commendable.

Robbery and Murder on East Sports Association Road 170

Xu Liu Xiang Died in the Night After Encountering Robbers

Xu Liu Xiang, a local resident living at 30 Di Jia Bang, East Sports Association Road, Jiangwan, is 44 years old and has been a craftsman at Gu Fali Foreign Company at 137 Sichuan Road for 15 years. He is usually cautious and reliable. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday (the 7th) at about 7:30 PM, he was having dinner at home when his close friend Zhang Xiangfa came to invite him to his house for dinner. Not long after, Zhang said goodbye because he was anxious to return, about twenty minutes later, Xu went out alone. When he was walking near Mao Quantai's factory on Caojia Bang, East Sports Association Road, unexpectedly several robbers flashed out of the darkness and blocked his way, intending to rob him. Xu Liu Xiang was strong and powerful and resisted the robbers, which caused him to be shot by the robbers, shot in the chest, a shot next to the left breast, two front teeth knocked out, and cut in several places on the face and body. There was also a rope tied around his neck, which showed that he had resisted the robbers violently at the time. Xu died of serious injuries on the spot. It was not until the next morning, at dawn, that passers-by saw the body and informed the family, and then they learned that Xu Liu Xiang had died. The family, together with the local security guards, reported to the No. 5 District 3 Public Security Bureau. At about 10:00 AM on the 9th, officials from the Landlord's Hall went to investigate, and the death was confirmed to be a robbery and murder. The family was instructed to collect the body themselves and wait for the arrest of the murderer for review and handling. After Xu's death, he left behind a wife and eight children, only the eldest daughter was married, and his situation was desolate. Xu Liu Xiang was robbed of a hat and thirty yuan in cash.

Grand Opening of China National Goods Company 174

China National Goods Company (Continental Commercial Building, Nanjing Road) opened yesterday. At 9:00 AM, before the door was opened, customers and congratulatory guests outside the door were already shoulder to shoulder, waiting eagerly for the opening.

The True Calligraphy of Song Wenxin, Duke of the State of Xin, Embodies the Great National Character of China 175

Exhibited publicly at the Ningbo Native Place Association on the 12th. A calligraphy piece personally written by Song Wenxin, Duke of the State of Xin, in the sixth year of Xianchun, featuring the sayings of Monk Hui, is several feet long. The calligraphy is well-preserved and contains inscriptions by famous figures throughout history, including Yuan Wang Meng, Ming Wen Zhengming, Wen Zhenshen, Qing Ye Shaoben, and Li Yanzhang. During the Daoguang era of the previous Qing dynasty, a certain traveling official encountered the Hui-Han War in Yunnan, which lasted for eighteen years. Somehow, the calligraphy piece ended up in the collection of Imperial Censor Luo Pingbao in Yunnan Province. Now, his descendant, Mr. Dou Shao Huai, who harbored ambitions since childhood and studied military affairs, during the September 18th Incident and the Songhu Battle, Mr. Dou delivered speeches in Yunnan, constantly encouraging the public to preserve the national territory and support the Northeast by aiding the volunteer army. He was recommended by the Yunnan Provincial Anti-Japanese Support Association to represent and comfort the volunteer army in the Northeast. Upon returning home and packing, he unintentionally discovered a calligraphy piece of Song Wenxin, Duke of the State of Xin, from the old collection of Imperial Censor Dou. He earnestly requested Mr. Chen Xiaopu of Kunming, the former Shandong Chief Education Officer (i.e., Chen 　Sou), to examine and verify it. Mr. Chen recognized it as a rare treasure, of great relevance to China's history and culture. He added an inscription to record the event. While leaving Yunnan and passing through Hong Kong, Mr. Hu Zhantang, the former President of the Legislative Yuan, appraised it and deemed it a valuable item. After arriving in Shanghai, he entrusted friends to seek detailed appraisal from famous figures in Beijing and Shanghai, including Xie Huisheng, Yang Cangbai, Sun Bolan, Chu Huiseng, Shi Liangcai, Li Dahao, and Shanren Shi Linghan. All considered it a national treasure, not suitable for individual preservation, and suggested it should be made public or preserved by the state, to inspire the spirit of the nation and save the precarious Republic of China. Mr. Dou deeply agreed. Starting from 1 PM to 5 PM on the 12th of this month, it will be exhibited for several days at the Ningbo Native Place Association on Xizang Road, participating in a calligraphy and painting exhibition. The tentatively set price is ten thousand yuan, with five thousand yuan earmarked for expenses for working in the Northeast. Regardless of the amount sold, the remaining proceeds will be donated to the volunteer army. Anyone who admires the great national character of Duke of the State of Xin and supports resisting Japan to save the country, please come and view it quickly.

The stream of visitors never ceased, and the threshold was worn through. It was truly the grandest scene since the establishment of the National Goods Company in Shanghai. Guests included Wang Xiaolai, Qin Runqing, Pan Gongzhan, Xu Peihuang, Bei Songsun, Wen Lanting, Qian Chengxu, Chen Pingcheng, Fang Jiyang, Pan Xulun, Guo Shun, Kuang Zhongmou, Xu Xinliu, Chu Huiseng, Chen Songyuan, Shi Jiu'ao, Zhang 　Bo, Fang Jiaobo, Jin Lüqin, Zou Bingwen, Jing Runshi, Shen Tianxin, Feng Shaoshan, Zhao Shuyong, Yu Zuoting, Lao Jingxiu, and over a thousand others. They were warmly received by Manager Fang Yexian, Deputy Manager Li Kangnian, Directors Shi Liangcai, Wang Zhixin, Cai Shengbai, Ren Shigang, Fang Jiange, Ye Youcai, Pan Yangyao, Zhang Huikang, Supervisors Gui Yanfang, and Cheng Nianpeng. The guests expressed great satisfaction with the company's extensive collection of domestic products and thorough inspection forms. On that day, customers received commemorative gifts and copies of the special opening issues of Shen Bao and Chen Bao. It is said that the total business volume for the day reached over fifty thousand gold yuan.

Human Trafficking Organization Uncovered in Xiangfen Lane 177

Zhang Hongdou Sentenced to Two Months, Suspended

The Chief Detective of the Old Zhabei Police Station recently received confidential information that a human trafficking organization was operating at No. 70 Xiangfen Lane, and that it was also harboring assassination suspects. Therefore, the detective, along with Detectives Liu Junqing and Zhou Guisen, rushed to the location for a raid the day before yesterday afternoon. Upon arrival, they found the double doors tightly closed. After knocking for a long time, a woman named Lin Wangshi opened the door. Detective You and others immediately detained the woman and an eleven-year-old girl named Zhang Aidi. Upon searching the house, Lin Wangshi's paramour, Lin Wenming, who was hiding under the bed, was also found and brought back to the police station. After questioning, it was learned that Aidi lived at No. 165 Zhengjia Wood Bridge in the French Concession with an elderly woman named Zhang Chenshi, who was nearly seventy years old. Zhang Chenshi had bought Aidi as an adopted daughter when she was six years old. Recently, Zhang Hongbao, a prostitute from the Heyi Lane No. 6 brothel on Guangxi Road, lured Aidi out and forced her into prostitution. Although Aidi was not yet an adult, she had been sexually involved with several men. Since Zhang Hongbao had deceived her and Aidi dared not return home, Zhang Hongbao housed her at Lin's residence. The detectives also learned that Lin Wenming, in December of last year, along with his accomplice Lu Xuedao, had abducted a young woman named Zhang Adou, who was just over a year old, at the Xian Shi Amusement Park and took her to a hotel for sexual relations. Later, Lu took her to a brothel in Tianjin, where she was sold for eighty yuan, which was then split between them. However, Lu is now missing and cannot be traced. Only Zhang Hongbao was arrested. Yesterday morning, along with the Lin Wenming couple, they were sent to the First Special District Local Court, and Aidi was summoned to testify. Judge Qian Hongye conducted the trial. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu explained the case and questioned Zhang Aidi, who stated that she had voluntarily received guests and was not forced. The Lin couple stated that Aidi was brought to their residence by Hongbao. Hongbao admitted to housing Aidi at Lin's residence. After the trial, Judge Qian sentenced Zhang Hongbao to two months in prison, suspended for two years due to being a first-time offender. Lin Wenming and Lin Wangshi were found not guilty in the Aidi case. As for the case of abducting Zhang Abao, it did not comply with the procedures and should not be accepted. Zhang Aidi was taken home by her family.

Reader Advisor

How Can We Complete Our Love? 178

丨Letter from Mr. Zhou丨

I have a difficult problem, please give me a clear instruction. I think you are very busy, so I’ll make it short: I am a high school student about to graduate. Although my family is not wealthy, my father and brothers are still earning a living, so we can manage. I am already twenty years old. My parents always tell me to resolve the issue of marriage early. In the past, they introduced me to many families, some with daughters from wealthy or powerful families. But I always felt that this kind of transactional system was not something I wanted to do. Therefore, my parents told me to handle this matter myself. But in this world obsessed with money, how can a poor scholar like me be qualified to talk about love? So, this matter has been put off until last year, and I always answered them with "Let's wait." But last summer vacation, a woman who I used to be in love with reignited our romance. In the past, people said she was a romantic, depraved, and extremely bad woman. Friends advised me not to get close to her again. My parents scolded me, saying that I shouldn't be so self-destructive. But I don't think she's that kind of person. Her past life was indeed very depraved, but it wasn't her fault. It was entirely because she was too young and was deceived by others. They shouldn't blame her. We should forgive her! No, we should sympathize with her. Now that she has realized her mistakes, how can we not help her? So, I made a big decision and immediately accepted her love. At the same time, she is very grateful to me, so our love has reached its highest intensity. However, our difficulties have also come with it. It turns out that her parents do not agree with our love. I realized this recently from their attitude towards her. Because in recent months, their surveillance of her has been very strict. All the letters I give her have to go through their strict inspection, and some are not even delivered to her (this has never happened before). This has made our feelings very distant. At the same time, I heard that my family, seeing that we have a close relationship, also wants to facilitate this good thing. They once asked someone to speak to her family. Although my father and her father have been friends for many years, they were turned away. So, this matter has been put off. From these two points, it is clear that her parents do not approve of our relationship. So, what should we do? Should we elope? But there is no way to get her out of her family because she is being watched. Should I ask my friends and relatives to plead again? The past facts have already told us the answer. What's the point of running into a wall again? Then, should I give her up? I would never do such a thing that goes against my conscience! But what should I do? There is another layer, can

Mr. have a way to get her out of her family's restraints? But how should we proceed with our future? What about the question? The question of living? Because my family has recently had discord between my brother and sister-in-law, and it will definitely break down soon. After the breakdown, wouldn't even my personal life be affected? How would I have the ability to support her then? Regarding this point,

Mr. might say: "If there is really no way, you can find work!" Yes! This is indeed a wonderful way out. But in this society where there are more people than jobs, how can it be so easy to find work? Moreover, we have no specialized skills. I am just a high school student, and she is just a graduate of a sericulture school. With the silk industry already bankrupt in China, there are no jobs for her. We have no powerful people, so how can we find our rice bowls? Of course, if we take off our robes and go underground to live like cattle and horses, there will be no shortage of work. But our bodies, which have long been spoiled by a life of leisure, how can we do that? So, these things definitely need to be considered before we proceed with this matter, don't you think? I have always admired the

Brilliant sir! You will surely be able to give me a perfect answer to these difficult questions. I am eagerly waiting!

Reply: After reading your letter, we have a lot of emotion. This emotion is not about the oppression of the old society, but rather that we Chinese youth lack the ability to be independent. Like you, before the love issue arose, you relied on your parents for a "life of leisure" and didn't feel anything lacking. But now, for the sake of love, you want to live independently, and you immediately feel all sorts of difficulties. This is a complete exposure of the weakness of youth's dependence! Although this is not the main point you asked us to answer, it is worth mentioning specifically and discussing with you. Then we will talk about the love issue: You can forgive her for being deceived by others, sympathize with her awakening, and decide to accept her love, breaking all prejudices. This kind of understanding is worthy of our approval. But I don’t know if the other party's awakening is real, and whether your observation of her is genuine, and whether there is anything concealed by emotions? You still need to consider this carefully. If your observation of her is indeed genuine, then this love is very easy to complete. According to what is said in the letter, your parents have agreed to this marriage, while the other parents are against it. This is quite strange; Since the other party has stumbled, it stands to reason that your parents should be the ones opposing this marriage. The other parents probably have something they don't want, but now it's the opposite, which is really a bit contrary to common sense. I don’t know what the other parents are against? That is, what is the reason for their opposition to this marriage? In this regard, you should go back and study it. Whatever the result of the study, whether it is reasonable or unreasonable, in this reasonable or unreasonable, you can always find a solution. This method is to kindly explain the misunderstanding of the other party's parents. If the other party's parents are stubborn to the end, then if you both ask yourself if you have the courage to fight society, at least have the ability to live independently, you may wish to leave the family and form a small family. According to the law, men and women who are of age (full 20 years old) can freely engage and marry, and no one may interfere. You don't have to be afraid of people oppressing you on this point. (However, you should pay attention to whether the other party has reached adulthood) The problem of life after leaving the family should naturally be thought of by yourself. If you are afraid of not finding a job temporarily, you can go to look for it before you actually live together. Wait until you find a definite occupation and there is no problem with life, then you can do it according to your purpose. You said that your body has been spoiled by a life of leisure, but that is just an excuse. Even if your body is not very strong, you will always be unable to do things. Even if you can't do hard work, ordinary and not very laborious things will not torture you. If you are fundamentally afraid of doing things and just want to rely on others to live, then you are simply not worthy of being a modern youth, and you are simply not worthy of talking about love, so you should listen to others! If you have the courage to fight society, then this basic independent life should have a way to make it happen. There are even greater difficulties in society waiting for you to open up. If you are timid and afraid of things everywhere, and defend yourself with the name "spoiled", you may not have hope for a lifetime. A strong physique and a brave spirit should be honed in hardship and difficulty. If you are afraid of honing, how can light come? Here, you should have some deep understanding! Here, the reporter believes that the important issue at present does not seem to be in the question of "how to complete", but in the question of "whether to complete", in other words: It is easy for you to succeed in love, but whether the other party is really lovely? Does she really love you? Will the future ending be satisfactory? You still need to do some research on these issues. Don't indulge in temporary emotions, and it will end up being a waste. This is what the reporter wants to say outside of the questions asked in the letter. I hope you will think carefully!

City Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan's Speech [Shanghai's Education] (2) 188

Overview of School Education and Social Education

Now, I will briefly report on the current situation of various levels as follows:

I. Kindergarten School education's first stage is kindergarten. Cultivating children is important. There are very few independently established kindergartens in the city. Most are attached to primary schools. Only the Municipal First Kindergarten is an independent kindergarten, founded in 1929. There are a total of twelve municipal kindergartens attached to primary schools. In addition, there are five private Li'an kindergartens, plus twenty private, unregistered ones, and the Shanghai Middle School Kindergarten of the Provincial Level, totaling twenty-nine kindergartens in the city. According to the 1931 statistics, these kindergartens had a total of 1,856 children and 110 teachers.

Most kindergartens in the city have one director who leads several teachers and nannies to share all teaching and management affairs. If the number of students is less than 50, they are organized into one classroom. If there are about 100 students, they are divided into two classrooms. The facilities in the kindergarten include various models and forms, instruments, pianos, toys, etc., required for games, music, work, knowledge, and decoration. Their curriculum is roughly divided into three parts: singing and playing, sports, and work. According to the children's needs, the project method is used to arouse the children's motivation, and then they are guided according to the situation, so that the children's physical and mental development can be properly developed.

Primary schools: The city has a dense population, and the number of school-age children should of course be extremely large. How many are there? According to the statistics of the second semester of 1931 (i.e., summer of 1932), there were only 624 schools, distributed as follows:

(1) National: 1, (2) Ministerial: 2, (3) Provincial: 1, (4) Municipal: 186, (5) Public Concession's Municipal Council: 8, (6) French Concession's Municipal Council: 1, (7) Other public: 3, (8) Private registered: 146, (9) Private unregistered: 276, Total: 624.

In terms of funding, according to the 1931-1932 statistics, the total funding for municipal primary schools in the city was 527,797 yuan, while the total funding for public and private primary schools in the city was 2,248,136 yuan. Compared with the 2,145,211 yuan in 1929-1930, it has increased by 102,925 yuan. In the winter of 1931, the total number of primary school children in the city was: (1) Boys: 80,111, (2) Girls: 33,493, totaling 113,604. The number of female students is almost half of the number of male students, which shows that women's education has also made much progress compared to the past. Speaking of the distribution of ages, the oldest student in the primary level is about 19 years old, and the youngest is 4 years old, while the oldest student in the complete primary school is 20 years old, and the youngest is 8 years old. According to the statistics of the first semester of 1931-1932, the total number of teachers was 4,787. On average, each teacher teaches 24 students. This ratio seems too small compared to Western countries. It can be seen that school facilities and teacher efficiency should be increased as much as possible, and it is hoped that at least 50 to 60 students can be assigned to one teacher.

As for the school's grade organization, most primary schools in the urban area have a large number of children entering the school, and more than 80% are single-grade organizations. There are also complex-grade organizations. More than 80% of rural primary schools are single-grade organizations, with a small number using complex-grade organizations, while single-grade organizations are rare. As for teaching methods, most middle and high grades use Japanese-style tutoring, and lower grades use project-based learning. In class teaching, attention is also paid to individual differences. In addition, the First Experimental Primary School was specially established. The Dalton system was tested the year before last, and life-based integrated education is being implemented this year.

Speaking of the situation of primary school graduates, it is also interesting. According to the statistics of 1930-1931, there were a total of 1,231 graduates from municipal primary schools in the city, of which 62.71% went on to higher education, 23.08% were employed, 18.61% were unemployed, and 5.60% were in other categories.

In addition, the primary school curriculum is all in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education. As for facilities, schools in the urban area are more complete than schools in the rural area. Almost all primary schools in the urban area have classrooms, workshops, meeting rooms, gymnasiums, school gardens, cooperatives, reading rooms, and fire and health facilities. Most schools have already installed them. Rural primary schools and private primary schools have slightly worse facilities than municipal schools in the urban area.

II. Secondary schools: Since there are more than 600 primary schools in the city, the demand for secondary schools is also extremely urgent. Although secondary schools in the city cannot be said to be developed, they are much more advanced than before. Now, the general situation is described as follows:

(A) Total number of secondary schools in the city: Secondary schools in the city are divided into two types: (1) Junior secondary schools: national 1, municipal 2, private registered 11, private unregistered 24, total 38. (2) Complete secondary schools (two levels): national 1, provincial 1, municipal 2, Municipal Council of the Public Concession 5, Municipal Council of the Public Concession 1, private registered 38, private unregistered 25, total 74.

(B) The total expenditure of secondary schools in the city is shown in the following table:

1929- 1931-

News from Various Schools 190

Shenmei Girls' High School After Shenmei Girls' High School moved to its new address on Maigen Road, the school buildings are spacious and the scale is grand. The internal organization strives for perfection. This semester, many specialized teachers in various subjects have been newly hired. They are all well-known people in the country and are currently engaged in inviting experts in various subjects in the country to give lectures in rotation every week to increase students' interest. Classes officially start on the 6th.

Bai'e Painting Tutoring School The Bai'e Painting Tutoring School affiliated to the Bai'e Painting Association, which is filed with the Ministry of Education and registered with the Shanghai Education Bureau, is the only painting tutoring school in Shanghai. Since moving to the Western-style house at No. 714, the intersection of Aiven Road and Kader Road, it has opened winter tutoring classes, and many people have joined. It is now known that the school's spring semester will officially start on January 15th, and registration will begin one week in advance. Recently, the number of applicants has been very enthusiastic. However, due to the limited school buildings, the school has decided to only accept 60 students each. No more will be accepted when the quota is full, regardless of gender. Anyone who is interested in studying art, whether they have studied it or not, can quickly register to join. In addition, the school recently added a practical fine arts crash course from 9:00 a.m. to 12:00 a.m. due to the lack of practical art talents in the current society and the requirements of various scholars. Whether you have a painting foundation or not, you can complete it within half a year, and use practical skills for production to meet the needs of the society. The class is personally taught by the famous painter Xue Hu, and the teaching is meticulous and detailed. The subjects are divided into four types: sketching (cartoons, satire books, advertising paintings, and decorative paintings, etc.), patterns (color, monochrome, crafts, and decorative patterns, etc.), painting (book cover paintings, advertisements, and various decorative paintings), and art writing (various writing methods in Chinese and Western languages). It is the only good opportunity for those who are limited by economic time but are uneasy about applied art. Exquisite details are available, and a four-point stamp is required for information.

Yangxing Primary School The private Yangxing Primary School on Datong Road, Zhabei, has been approved by the Municipal Education Bureau to conduct a trial run. The number of students in the current semester has increased sharply by nearly a hundred. Yesterday, the school held an opening ceremony. More than a hundred teachers, students, parents, and guests attended. The school principal Tang Kejia, teachers Zhang Jizhi and Zhang Ai, and school board representative Sun Yucai reported on the school's future improvement plans and expansion plans. The students' parents were very satisfied. There are still vacancies in the school's various grades.

Jinan National Arts Performance 191

And will run a broadsword training class

(Jinan, 9th) Today, the Second Route Army's National Arts Team and the students of the Provincial National Arts Museum, a total of more than 500 people, performed national arts at the Qianfoshan Sports Field. The sword shadows and sword lights were extremely exciting. Thousands of people participated, including several Japanese officers who expressed their admiration. The event ended at 3 o'clock. A dinner was held at the Jinde Association. Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun gave a speech on behalf of Han Fuju, encouraging them to continue their efforts, strengthen their bodies, and save the country. The Provincial National Arts Museum believes that in the face of national crisis, public sports are important. It has decided to open 17 broadsword training classes in Jinan, with 40 people in each class. After graduating in six months, recruitment will continue, and the National Arts Museums in various counties and cities will also be ordered to open and set up public national arts practice factories. It is also planned to hold a provincial national arts examination in April to promote it.

Badminton Competition Rules and Methods (Below)

(V) General Rules 200

(12) The receiver of the ball shall continue to serve the ball. In the same game, one person cannot have two consecutive serves.

(13) The server shall not serve the ball until the opponent is ready. However, if the opponent attempts to return the ball, it shall be deemed as ready.

(14) The side that starts the game first shall only have one serve in the first week. In subsequent weeks, each side's pairing shall have one serve. The two sides' pairings shall serve in succession.

(15) The server and receiver must stand in their respective halves of the court (bounded by the front service line, back service line, and sidelines). Before the ball is served, a part of the body must be in contact with the ground.

(16) The following shall be considered a [re-serve]: if the ball touches the net when serving, assuming it would otherwise be a legal serve. However, touching the net during the game shall not be re-served. If the return of the ball passes outside the net post and lands within the boundary of the opponent's court, it shall be considered a legal return. If the umpire considers there to be an unexpected obstruction, he may order a re-serve.

(17) If a player serves the ball from the wrong half of the court and scores a point, assuming a request for a re-serve is made or granted before the next serve, then a re-serve shall be granted.

(18) If a player serves the ball while standing in the wrong half of the court, and that player's side wins the point, assuming a request for a re-serve is made or granted before the next serve, then a re-serve shall be granted.

(Note) If a player changes halves and serves from a half of the court that they should not change to, and this error is only discovered after the next serve, then this error shall stand, and a re-serve cannot be requested or granted.

(19) The umpire's responsibilities: if he discovers a foul or a ball that requires a re-serve, he shall immediately call it out without requiring the player to tell him. If there is a dispute before the next serve, he shall resolve it immediately. If necessary, he may also appoint linesmen. In matches where umpires are appointed, the umpire's decision shall be final. However, in matches where a referee is appointed, only the umpire's decisions on matters of law may be requested for joint resolution.

(VI) Singles 201

(20) In matches where one player plays against one player on each side, the above rules shall also apply, except in the following circumstances:

(A) When the server's score is zero, both players, server and receiver, must be in the right half of the court. If, in a match, the cumulative score is odd, then the serve and the receiving, both must be on the left hand.

(B) After each player scores a point, they must switch halves of the court. The next consecutive serve must be received by the same player.

(C) Women's singles matches are a total of eleven points. If the score is nine points each, the side that scores nine points first has the right to call for an end to the set and re-determine the winner with five points. If each side scores ten points, the side that scores ten points first has the right to call for an end to the set and determine the winner with three points.

[P (VII) Problematic Points>

The following is an attachment to the ball rules, approved by the Bamingdun Association:

(1) If the server does not hit the ball when intending to serve, it shall not be counted as a foul or error. However, if the racket touches the ball, then regardless of weight, the rules regarding serving shall be effective.

(2) If A serves the ball to B, and the ball touches B's partner, or is intended to be hit, even if they are standing outside the court, A shall be awarded a point.

(3) If a player touches the ball during the game (if not for a legal return) or is touched by the ball, it shall be counted as a failure, regardless of whether they are standing inside or outside the boundaries of the court.

(4) If the ball touches the top of the net and passes over when serving, and is hit by the opposing player, then the ball shall be considered otherwise falling in the proper court, it is on this basis according to ball regulations 16, get weight hair, not for the violations of the rules.

(5) During the game, the ball falls into the net or outside the court, or the opposing player's body or racket touches the net, shall not be punished because the ball is not [in, during the competition], (See ball regulations, article 10 has)

(6) [Player], the two words, from one post after the ball is serving to say is in the competition.

(7) If a player gets a killing chance when they are near the net, the other player raises the racket next to the net, attempting to make the ball bounce back on the racket. The said measure to the ball regulation, Article 10 Ren's obstruction,

But a player can use the racket to protect the face, if does not obstruct the opponent, (End)

Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team

丨Outline of the Tour of Europe and America Plan丨 202

Funding: National currency 94,000 yuan

Route: Around the earth

Number of people: A group of twelve

Duration: Estimated seven months

The Liangjiang Women's Basketball Team is preparing for a tour of Europe and America. The news has been repeatedly reported by various Chinese and foreign newspapers in this city. Now the outline of the plan is recorded as follows:

Name: China Shanghai Liangjiang Girls' School Tour of Europe and America Basketball Team

Purpose: ㈠ Promote the spirit of the Chinese nation, connect with the feelings of women around the world, and enhance China's international status. ㈡ Observe the status of education and sports facilities around the world as a reference for the implementation of sports in China.

Organization: The team is organized by teachers and students of Liangjiang Girls' School. The entire team consists of twelve people. Their duties are listed as follows: ㈠ One main person (i.e., the leader) directs all team affairs. ㈡ One secretary handles translation and communication. ㈢ One coach is responsible for training techniques and managing team members. ㈣ Nine team members, including one team captain and one secretary each.

Route: Depart from Shanghai, go to the Philippines, cross the Pacific Ocean to San Francisco, through Chicago to New York and Boston, then cross the Atlantic Ocean to London, Marseille, and various European cities, then to the South Pacific islands and return to Shanghai, which is a circumnavigation of the Earth. (The formalities for going abroad will be handled by Zhu Shaoping, President of the Global Student Association.)

Duration: This team's trip is a circumnavigation of the Earth. It will depart in mid-March of the 22nd year. It will stay in the United States and its territories for about one month, in various parts of Europe for about two months, and in the South Pacific islands for about one month. Including travel time, the total time will be about seven months, and it is expected to return around mid-September, limited to one semester.

Budget: The team's budget proposal will be planned by China Travel Service before departure, according to the most economical group travel budget for world tour groups. The boat and train fare per person is estimated to be 1,500 Chinese yuan, which is about 30,000 yuan for twelve people. The food and accommodation costs per person are estimated to be at least 2,000 yuan, which is 24,000 yuan for twelve people. However, if the price of gold decreases, it may be slightly reduced. (The funding reasons will be handled by Yan Shuhe, President of Shanghai Women's Bank.)

Selection of personnel: The team's staff and members, in addition to having expertise, rich knowledge, and being physically strong and of good character, must also have great aspirations and be qualified to represent the spirit of the nation. (Before going abroad, Dr. Niu Huisheng, Director of the Orthopedic Hospital, will conduct a physical examination on their behalf.)

Competition: Focus on friendly matches with various groups and schools as a principle. The matters concerning contacting competitions will be handled by Mr. Shen Siliang, Chief Secretary of the Chinese National Sports Association.

Accommodation: The accommodation in each place should be economical, hygienic, and suitable for women. Therefore, the YWCA in various places is tentatively designated as the accommodation. As for the contact, Ms. Shu Jing, General Secretary of the National YWCA of China, will handle it on their behalf.

Clothing: The entire team is required to wear uniformly elegant styles and use the best quality domestic goods as materials to show patriotism. The following is specified: ㈠ Sports clothing: The upper body is made of domestically produced pure white spun silk to highlight the team name and number of the short shirt, and the lower body is hidden in woolen shorts, with white stripes, and white sneakers. The color is simple and mainly emphasizes healthy beauty. ㈡ Casual clothing: Wear short-cut shirts and skirts, fully presenting the elegance and health of Chinese female students. ㈢ Formal wear: Purely Chinese, the most beautiful and solemn attire, to show the inherent art of the East.

Copper Coins Suddenly Retreated

The situation yesterday will be distributed as follows:

Foreign Exchange Slackens 214

The afternoon market had no opportunity for a meeting as usual, and trading will not begin until today. [Silver Loans] Because the needs of all sectors are still weak and there are few uses, there seems to be no possibility of tight silver funds. In the end, it was still the same as before, all borrowed for free. The small general meeting also opened a free draw for the first lot.

Auxiliary Coins Contract and Expand 215

Jiangnan small silver dollars, in view of the excessive decline in Guangdong angle dollars, also followed suit and decreased. Yesterday, it fell 4.5 hairs, to 6 qian 2 fen 3 hairs, and the transaction was still limited, at 6500 angles. Guangdong small silver dollars, after falling the day before yesterday, rose slightly by 7 hairs and 5 silks yesterday, to 5 qian 9 fen 1 hair 7 silks and 5 hairs, with a transaction of 75,000 angles. Copper coins contracted sharply, suddenly contracting by 3,500 wen from the day before yesterday, to 418,500 wen. The transaction also decreased, to only over 51,000 strings, with a total price of 12,200 taels of silver.

Inflow and Outflow of Silver and Dollars 216

[Silver Funds] Yesterday, the bank's receipts and settlements increased compared to the past. Chinese merchants' receipt and settlement bills were over 2.0 million, foreign merchants' receipt and settlement bills were 1.78 million, telegraphic transfers were over 700,000, loans were over 1.4 million, and bank receipts and settlements were over 3.0 million. Silver deposit transactions were over 1.1 million, and various goods, exchange taxes, and other receipts and settlements were 6.45 million. 800,000 were taken out of the warehouse, and money shops and silver public single receipts and settlements were over 27 million. Drawdown receipts and settlements were over 3.5 million, and various other receipts were over 500,000. 670,000 was received in cash. [Dollar Funds] Exchange draws, 940,000 were made in the morning market. Transactions in the note market were 64,000 inside the market and 85,000 outside the market. Bank check transactions were 35,000. As usual, the afternoon market did not have a meeting, and there was nothing to record. Bank buying and selling of dollar funds was 1.05 million, and receipts and settlements between dollar accounts of various banks were over 1.7 million. Note cancellations, inflows, and outflows were over 1.5 million, and dollar deposit transactions were over 600,000. Money shop and dollar public single receipts and settlements were over 4.6 million. Dollar drawdown receipts and settlements were over 1.8 million, and dollar loans were over 1.3 million. Small money shop transactions were over 600,000.

Financial Circles Send Out Visiting Cards 217

On the money shop side, every year before the Lantern Festival, for five or six days, visiting cards are sent out to customers. As a rule, only real customers and employees with connections are likely to be approved. Now, due to changes in current affairs, the opposite is true. Money shops, in order to be cautious in their operations and avoid danger, are reluctant to send out cards indiscriminately. In the end, there are quite a few who open the cards but dare not send them out. As for those who have already sent them out, they have only reached about one-third. This is a general overview of the opening and sending of cards in the past five or six days. As for the bank side, in recent years, they have not only been engaged in banking business as before. Now, they are also engaged in money shop-like lending business and are also asking employees to solicit business in various ways. Although banks such as the Bank of Communications and the Bank of Communications do not do this at their headquarters, all branches have this major plan for operation. Therefore, most of the important business of money shops has now been robbed by banks.

Fluctuations in Securities and Bond Markets 218

Yesterday, the public debt market of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was slightly more active, and trading also increased slightly. However, market prices still rose and fell erratically, and the range of fluctuation became narrower and narrower. Market sentiment was still due to the lack of progress in the diplomatic situation. Supply and demand were quite balanced. Trading was more energetic in the two morning sessions. In the first session, retail investors bought quite a bit, and Nos. 11 and 32 were also bought a bit. Market prices increased by 34 cents. In the second session, long positions were swapped, and there were several signs of low near-term and high deferred positions. Trading was lighter in the afternoon, and market prices fluctuated without certainty, generally fluctuating between 12 cents. Major players did not come on the market to buy or sell. The market price results were mixed, with some rising and some falling. Among them, reorganization bonds fell slightly by 2 cents, salt tax bonds fell slightly by 1 cent and 5 hairs, and the rest rose slightly by 23 cents. The total number of transactions was 5,079,000 yuan, of which 4,000 yuan was in spot goods, and salt tax futures accounted for more than 3.5 million yuan. The rest ranged from 230,000 to 500,000 yuan. Only 18 customs bonds and Jin Chang 96 bonds each traded for 5,000 yuan.

Yarn Flower Prices Drop, The Wind of Decline Gradually Rises 220

Indian Cotton Opens at 2,000 Pieces, Price Drops Another 7.5 Cents

The yarn market is becoming weak, and the wind of decline is gradually intensifying. Because it has been brewing and fluctuating for a long time, customer sales are still stagnant, and market sentiment is weak, and scattered long positions are showing anxiety. In addition, the cotton market is unstable, and the yarn market, which is closely related, is even more difficult to stabilize. As for the real demand, because the commercial situation in the interior is depressed, it is difficult to improve for a while. In addition, the smoke of war is thick in North China. It can still be maintained for the time being. If spot yarn is suspended for a long time, there will be a drastic change.

Human Mark Drops Two Over 221

The Human Mark market opened in the morning, with American cotton stable and Indian cotton very weak, which softened market sentiment, and selling pressure was stronger. Prices for each month fell 4, 5, 6, 7, and 8 cents. In the afternoon, there were reports of cheap Indian cotton being made to order, and the market situation was even weaker. Prices for each month fell another 4, 5, 6, and 7 cents. The total transaction for the day was 19,800 bales. Grain: River-Bottom Rice Market Continues to Decline by Two to Three Jiao 226

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, there were 20 to 30 shipments from the river-bottom. Sales were sluggish. Package deals were disastrously low due to prices in other regions. Merchants were unwilling to buy much, with only 300-400 shi being traded. The market was quiet, and transactions were scarce. Sutung and South Port Qing rice fell slightly by two to three jiao. Changbang and Duyangjian followed suit with a decrease of one to two jiao. Standard silver dollars remained stable. No factory goods were traded.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, all river-bottom groups had over ten shipments. White polished rice sales were sluggish. Those that cut prices sold a little better. The market price dropped slightly by one to two jiao. The arrival of thin paddy rice was limited, and sales were flat. The market price remained constant. There were a few retail sales of early rice at a slightly lower price. The arrival of Dugu tips was limited, and sales were sluggish. The market price was stable. The arrival of Yangjian continued, but sales were slack. The market price was weak by about one chi. Silver dollars were stable. White dollars were down slightly by two to three jiao. Premium customers were sluggish.

More Arrivals of Ke Xian Than Sales 227

Yesterday, Ke Xian rice continued to arrive, and a small number of Ke Yuan also arrived in Shanghai. Statistics show there were another 4,000 to 5,000 bags. Due to the unstable situation and poor financial conditions, cargo owners mostly wanted to sell quickly. Although there were local and Minbang groups continuing to purchase, arrivals exceeded sales, and prices continued to fall by about five fen. Ke Yuan and Min-style substitutes were still active, and the market could temporarily stabilize. Because of consecutive days of decline, later arrivals could be reduced, and Min-style sales were becoming smoother. The local market traded 150 bags of Hunan oil rice at 8.65 yuan per bag. 823 bags of late Jiangxi machine rice were traded at 8.89 yuan per bag. The Minbang group purchased 454 bags of Wuhu machine rice from the weeds at 9.80 yuan to 9.50 yuan per bag. 50 bags of Nanjing machine rice were traded at 9.75 yuan per bag. 700 bags of Hunan machine red unfinished rice were traded at 8.56 yuan per bag, and 200 bags of late Jiangxi machine rice were traded at 8.90 yuan per bag. It is thought that future market activity from local buyers might lead to a return to level prices, but with too much rice stored in production areas, or continued shipments, the market price is difficult to predict.

The Miscellaneous Grains Market Still Lacks the Ability to Advance 228

Yesterday, sales of interior yellow soybeans in carload lots were seen. However, the market situation showed little improvement. In short, cake sales have not surged, and the oil market is weak. Therefore, everyone is eager to sell. However, inventories are not thick, and the market is slightly firmer within the weakness. Green beans saw balanced arrivals and sales, and the market situation was somewhat established. The Ningbo group purchased 600 bags of Gaoyou green beans. 1,500 bags of black beans were traded, down 7 fen, purchased by the Guangdong group. Mung beans remained weak, and high-quality goods continued to sell. The rest were generally flat and weak.

Yesterday's sugar market was stable as the silver price and Dutch exchange rate did not fluctuate much. Flour Noodle Prices on the Zhabei Cargo Line Turn Upward 231

Recently, the arrival of Longkou flour has become scarce, and the quoted price has been trending upward. It is now being gradually released at a price of 18 taels and 6 qian to 4 or 5 qian, an increase of 5 or 6 qian compared to before. Traded prices had been over 18 taels and 3 qian and have now followed suit. Yantai flour is being offered at 14 taels and 5 qian, with trade at the same price, showing a somewhat tight situation. Furthermore, according to a letter from Yantai, it is currently the time when the new crop is not yet available, and the local price is expected to rise.

Hardware: Tinplate Fixed Prices Rise by One to Two Shillings Strongly 232

Yesterday, hardware trading in this port showed slight improvement compared to the previous day. Among the buyers, the Yangtze River Group was the most active, and the Tianjin and Qingdao Groups were also quite strong. However, the Fujian and Guangdong Groups were still less active. The main offerings were from local factories, with the most common types being ingots, tinplate, galvanized iron sheets, and British steel plates, among others. New lead wire and galvanized iron sheets were also offered. Local factory ingots opened at 6 taels and 5 fen on the Japanese street, with an additional 5 qian for export via the Besshi process. 90-pound tinplate from England was estimated at 13 taels, 1 qian higher than before; 200-pound tinplate was 26 taels, 5 qian higher than before. Other goods saw little fluctuation. However, according to an incoming foreign telegram, yesterday's fixed price for tinplate rose again by 1 shilling to 3 shillings and 6 pence. For example, 90-pound English goods were 17 shillings and 4 pence per case, 100-pound were 18 shillings and 2 pence, 90-pound double-jointed iron was 34 shillings and 8 pence, and 100-pound double-jointed iron was 36 shillings. It is said that industry peers had no transactions.

Free Talk

Chats from the Violet Hut 256

— Shou Juan

No matter which country's literary writers and novelists, it is not uncommon to be a nationally famous literary writer or novelist. It is rare and valuable to become a world-renowned literary writer or novelist. Maxim Gorky of Russia is one of the world-renowned literary writers and novelists of the present era. The Russian people respect and adore him even more than Stalin, who is in charge of the national regime. His pen is truly mightier than ten million spears. Gorky is indeed a pen name; his real name is Peshkov, which few people know. However, the name Gorky is well-known to every household. His hometown is Nizhny Novgorod. His birthday is March 14, 1868; he is exactly sixty-five years old this year. He has held many professions in his life and often changed them, breaking all records for literary writers and novelists. According to the items in his autobiography: In 1878, he became an apprentice shoemaker. In 1879, he became an apprentice painter. In 1882, he worked as a dishwasher on a steamer. In 1883, he became a baker. In 1884, he was a gatekeeper for others. In 1885, he returned to baking. In 1886, he became a singer in a band. In 1887, he was an apple peddler. In 1888, because he became impatient with life, he joined a suicide society and prepared to commit suicide. In 1891, he worked as a lawyer's clerk. In 1892, with nothing to do, he became an unemployed vagrant, traveling all over Russia. In 1893, he worked as a worker on the railway. Seeing all his experiences, it is like the oral performance of the Su Tan singers of our country, the wandering rogue who abandoned ten professions. However, he has thus become knowledgeable and finally became a literary writer and novelist who is good at writing about the suffering of the common people. His articles are written with the tip of his pen dipped in his own blood, sweat, and tears. In 1894, he began to publish his first short stories, and later he made many novels, short stories, and plays, filled with compassion between the lines, so he is still an authority in the new Russian literary world. I have translated two of his short stories: 1: [Green Cat], 2: [Ill-fated Woman].

— Portrait of Gorky in his prime

Urban Sketches 257

— Guo Lanxin

A serious national crisis is unfolding before us, but the people in the city are still living a life of drunken stupor as if in a dream. Everyone believes that the sound of guns and cannons in the northeast border is not as tense and frightening as the Battle of Shanghai last year. Therefore, the national crisis remains a national crisis, and I continue to enjoy myself. Now let's go on a pilgrimage to the dance halls.

In the dance halls of Shanghai, the music is loud, the dancers are numerous, the lights are bright, and the alcohol flows. In such intoxicating places of enjoyment, many patriotic people who are enthusiastic about saving the country are found. During the day, they made passionate and慷慨speeches, but that's all they were. At night, they are buried in the places they condemned during the day. Ah, what a great contradiction!

In the Grand LaFayette Garden, several comrades who advocate saving the country through dancing were found. I don't believe that holding a soft and warm jade embrace, following the melody of the gentle sound, and dancing on the smooth floor, isolated from the outside world full of hunger, cold, poverty, can save the country through entertainment?

In the Moon Palace, in the Great East, in the New New, which place retains the shadow of the national crisis, which place holds the indignation of saving the country? A bird's nest in a dangerous building, fish swimming in a boiling pot. Continuing to enjoy ourselves like this, the great Republic of China will easily perish. Things must first rot before worms grow; people must first insult themselves before others insult them; a country must first attack itself before others attack it. May the people who enjoy themselves examine these words with their conscience!

Southeast Wind 258

— Sleeping Buddha

The northwest wind is what saves the country, while the southeast wind only destroys it!

I say this not because I am crazy, but because my feelings are too deep. I have seen the ice freezing on the river this time. A few days ago, the northwest wind blew like a hammer and scissors day and night, and the thermometer naturally dropped to zero. Although this gift from the northwest wind is incomparable to the bloody battles of our volunteer soldiers outside the customs, it is still enough for the people of Jiangnan, who are accustomed to warmth, to endure. However, we can feel interest while shivering, especially the children, because the water in the ten-foot-wide ditch has frozen into an inch of ice, which looks like a large mirror. Unfortunately, there are no young men and women in the style of Beiping here, except for the innocent children competing in races on the ice. Otherwise, this exhilarating ice skating will surely create a new record. The northwest wind keeps blowing, and the ice keeps freezing. The ships are all parked on the shore, unable to move for one day, two days, three days. The sun, which illuminates the earth, exerts its heat as much as possible, but it has never damaged it in the slightest! On the morning of the fourth day, the wind still came from the northwest, and the water source naturally taught people to look at it with new eyes. Suddenly, the sun seemed to retreat in shame, but the upper layer of the ice showed a patch of oily color, like a beauty with tears in her eyes. In the afternoon, it quietly disintegrated. By the time dusk was dim, the sound of oars was sent into the eardrums in bursts. It turned out that from ten o'clock that day, the northwest wind changed to the southeast wind. The cold remained the same, but the ice was all blown by the southeast wind to the land of nothing without resistance. While the sun was blushing and setting, it proudly radiated ten thousand rays of golden light, seemingly deliberately boasting its victory to the earth, and it was not ashamed to take the beauty of others.

Spinning horse lanterns, lion lanterns, airplane lanterns are even more exquisite and beautiful in the hands of several modern girls. Pairs of lovers strolled on Guanqian Street at dusk, crowded together, carrying Ye Shouhe's pastries and Caizhizhai's melon seeds... Is this a good phenomenon in Suzhou?

[Going out to aid] [Ready to fight with spears as pillows] [Volunteering to kill the enemy] [Advancing forward with a crossbow] [Armed resistance] [Recovering lost territory] [……] [……] This is equivalent to ice, condensed by the northwest wind and eliminated by the southeast wind.

[Old North Wind] is truly worthy of its name. The southeast wind, which is good at management, will also sigh here that its skills are exhausted. Even if it were given wings, it would not fly a step out of the customs, break through the northwest wind's barrier, and dream even more about it!

The northwest wind is what saves the country, while the southeast wind only destroys it!

— Huo Xueming

Looking around the Central Plains, how many military officers are not afraid of death? Crossing the border pass with weapons, leading the entire battalion of warriors to become martyrs.

Sketches of Wumen 260

— Bo Guang

The magnificent Xuanmiao Temple in the style of a palace always has a fluctuating crowd flowing in and out every afternoon. There are crane-like handsome men, snake-like charming women, and even little sisters and little brothers... Crowded! Fluctuating! Bustling, but it actually benefits the dim sum shops, grocery stalls, magic tricks, Suzhou operas, porcelain shops, bird shops... Women dig in their leather bags, and men grope around their bodies. Walking out of the temple gate, beggars nail themselves behind them, calling out to ladies, young ladies, young mistresses, young masters, but they are reluctant to take out a copper coin!

The [Journey to the West] scenery is really good, and the film of The Comedy of Marriage is also good. The prices of both places are very cheap. Get drunk, get drunk in the theater, in the cinema. Have you seen the shocking Sino-Japanese comparison in the YMCA? Have you seen the lack of material assistance for the Northeast Volunteer Army?

Photograph 261

— Mo Yi

After another burst of gunfire, bullets, as always, rained down on them. Then came another series of groans, sorrows, and hums. Bright red blood flowed, flowed, flowed, flowed incessantly...

Da... Da da... Da da da... Da da da da da da da... Da da da da da da... Da da da da da... Da da da da da da da... Da da da... Da da... Da...

Zhang Rongji seemed to hear a command, and the machine gun stopped firing.

[Ha... Haha... Hahahaha...]

[Ha... Haha... Hahahaha...]

In a burst of leather shoes, there was a burst of crazy laughter.

[This kid is not dead yet, he's moving, give him a bayonet!]

[This kid is still humming, come, give him a bayonet too!]

[Ah... Ah... Ah... Ah]

[Yo... Yo... Yo... Yo]

Several people who were not dead from the bullets were now stabbed a few more times with bayonets and involuntarily let out miserable exclamations; then they fell silent: they were probably all dead.

[This guy is covered in blood, really beautiful in red!... Hey, that's strange, how come this guy doesn't have any holes in him!...]

Zhang Rongji first felt that there were two people standing beside him, and then he suddenly felt lighter on his body. He understood that the people who were pressing on him had all been kicked away by the enemy. After a while, his legs were replaced by two feet, and he heard the enemy say these words. He thought, [Alas, it's over, there's no way I can live...] (9)

Miscellaneous Words

Nine-Flavor Tea Shop Zhang 262

— Yi An

The clay figurines of Wuxi are indeed good, at least they are delicate and concise, with strong contrast in colors, which easily attracts the attention of children. The faces of the sculpted children are all cute, and they are typical appearances of children in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang regions: narrow eyes, long eyebrows, round and prominent faces, grinning smiles, but it is a pity that the faces of every child made by every family are exactly the same. If the effect of education also becomes like this, then mankind can truly be driven by machines.

I had passed through Wuxi many times before, and each time I recognized it as Wuxi because of the many chimneys. I thought that once I arrived in Wuxi, I would be in a forest of chimneys, and I would inevitably have to worry about walking around the chimneys in circles. It wasn't until I actually arrived in Wuxi that I was relieved that there weren't as many chimneys as I had expected, although they could be seen everywhere.

Huiquan water is about half a cent higher than the cup's edge without overflowing, which is said to be a miracle. Later, we tried pouring their tea into cups at a restaurant on Wanqian Road, and it was also about half a cent above the edge of the cup without overflowing. The restaurant did not use Huiquan water. However, you can still argue like this: this is still Wuxi water after all. Back in Shanghai, I poured a full cup of tea, and it could be about half a cent above the edge of the cup without overflowing in the same way. According to them, Huiquan water has a higher amount of iron and is heavier in volume than water from other places. I think it may be true that the water quality is different from other places, but it may not have much to do with whether it overflows or not.

Near Huiquan, there is a small square pond, about three or four feet square and three or four feet deep. Tourists throw copper coins down, because the copper coins do not sink straight to the bottom, but must go down in a zigzag line, so they admit that the water here is magical. After the tourists throw the copper coins down, they certainly do not pick them up, because showing stinginess is a small matter, but irreverence towards this sacred spring is a big matter. I remember that there is also one in Longjing or Hupao in Hangzhou, and there is also a small pond on top of Taoguang where people throw copper coins into it like this. As for why the copper coins do not accumulate so much that they fill up and who cleans them up, it is an incomprehensible matter. Today, as I write this passage at home, thinking about it, I put down my pen, took two copper coins, filled a bucket with tap water, and after the water ripples stopped, I dropped the two copper coins one by one. The zigzag sinking situation was not much different from the shadows of the famous mountains and holy springs. The famous scenic spots and historical sites must always maintain a little mystery to be interesting. It is a bit煞风景 for me to stubbornly expose them like this, sin sin! At this point, I should recite [Namo Amitabha] three hundred times.

Basic English of 850 Words 263

A famous British psychologist and ethicist, Professor Ogden of Cambridge University, invented a basic English. This basic English only needs 850 words. The inventor firmly believes that these 850 words are sufficient for all applications. If foreigners can learn these 850 words and some simple sentence structure methods, they can use English freely and without obstacles. Among the 850 words, there are 600 nouns, including concrete and abstract ones; 150 adjectives; and 100 other miscellaneous words. Among these 100 miscellaneous words, there are only 14 verbs. In order to prove the possibility of this basic English, Ogden used these 850 words to narrate the entire famous work The Gold Bug by Edgar Allan Poe, and the result was extremely fluent. In this basic English, there is no word [fly], so it is replaced by [go into the air]; there is no word [shout], so it is replaced by [say loudly]; there is no word [sing], so it is replaced by [make sweet sounds], etc. It is easier than our country's Civilian Thousand Character Lesson.
